* The War

** 2022-12-16 Friday
- Near Svatove, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1603817323869089797][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.4794448,37.889303,11z][Stelmakhivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.5222553,37.9480571,13z][Novoselivske]]
- Near Kreminna, the Russians attacked Ploshchanka, Chervonopopivka, Bilohorivka, and Hryhorivka

** 2022-12-15 Thursday
- Near Svatove, Russian sources [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1603442647233806336][report]] ongoing Ukrainian attacks against [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.5222553,37.9480571,13z][Novoselivske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1314083,38.1373012,11z][Chervonopopivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.6277504,38.0248431,11z][Sofiivka]]
- Near Kreminna, Ukrainian forces [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1603442656104763393][continue to attack]] south of [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.995738,38.098652,11z][Dibrova]]
- Russian forces are [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1603442656104763393][reportedly attacking]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271478,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]] from the south
- More fighting [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1603442656104763393][was reported]] near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8603853,38.1878152,11z][Verkhnokamyanske]]
- Near Bakhmut ([[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1603442665659715585][1]], [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1603442674916376586][2]])
  - Russia attacked [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7145913,38.1364423,11z][Yakolivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6969475,38.0538431,11z][Soledar]]
  - Ukraine reportedly counterattacked near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7329344,38.2110851,11z][Bilohorivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6969475,38.0538431,11z][Soledar]]
  - Russian forces also attacked [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4682884,37.9557667,11z][Kurdyumivka]]
- Near Donetsk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1603442686295359488][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.746171,38.1475132,11z][Vesele]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9147295,37.4588834,11z][Pobjeda]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.8534122,37.4742253,11z][Novomykhailivka]]
- In Zaporizhzhia, the Ukrainian military [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1603442696110018560][struck targets]] in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.4716287,36.2285663,11z][Polohy]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.2489702,35.685411,11z][Tokmak]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@46.7177338,36.7154093,11z][Berdyansk]]
- A [[https://twitter.com/J_JHelin/status/1603363429594431489][thread]] on why the Russians are attacking Bakhmut
  - Bakhmut controls major highways running towards Slovyansk
  - Controls a rail line towards occupied Luhansk
  - Capturing Bakhmut makes it more difficult for Ukraine to hold Siversk
  - The terrain behind Bakhmut is more conducive to offensive maneuvers
  - Russia will likely launch a major offensive aimed at capturing Bakhmut in the spring
  - The overall goal of this offensive will be to capture the remainder of Donetsk Oblast
- There is an [[https://twitter.com/KofmanMichael/status/1603440911643557900][inconsistency]] between the Russian mobilization and the lack of production of artillery ammunition
  - Unlikely that Russian can restore offensive potential
  - Most likely that mobilized units will be used for defensive purposes and the consolidation of existing gains
- /The Economist/ has interviews with [[https://www.economist.com/ukraines-fateful-winter][President Zelensky]], [[https://www.economist.com/zaluzhny-profile][Gen. Zalhuzny]], and [[https://www.economist.com/syrsky-interview][Gen. Syrsky]]
  - Do not underestimate Russia
  - The mobilization indicates that Russia is in the fight for the long haul
  - Worries about supplies and ammunition
- Ukrainian forces [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1603432041550417923][hit a hotel]] in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@46.1223164,32.281866,11z][Zalizniy Port]], occupied Kherson, that was reportedly being used to house FSB personnel
- Drone footage showcasing the [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1603244522712236032][destruction]] of [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.554042,38.012325,11z][Opytne]], near Bakhmut
- A Russian ammunition depot in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.5969595,38.5740917,11z][Irmino]], Luhansk Oblast, [[https://twitter.com/Osinttechnical/status/1603523708534296576][has exploded]]
- [[https://twitter.com/Osinttechnical/status/1603456219250888706][Urban combat in Bakhmut]], filmed by Ukrainian forces
- The amount of Russian activity in Belarus [[https://rochan-consulting.com/issue-221-14-december-2022/][remains low and consists mostly of units moving to training facilities]]

** 2022-12-14 Wednesday
- [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1603007682146869248][Heavy fighting]] in the outskirsts of Bakhmut
- Near Kupyansk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1603077303415603201][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.8410201,37.7012762,12z][Hryanykivka]]
- Near Svatove, [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1603077312919969792][fighting is ongoing]] near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.5222553,37.9480571,13z][Novoselivske]], and Russian sources report fighting near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.4794448,37.889303,11z][Stelmakhivka]]
- Near Kreminna and Siversk, Russian forces [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1603077346025648128][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1314083,38.1373012,11z][Chervonopopivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9411955,38.1537086,11z][Serebryanka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271478,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]]
- Near Bakhmut, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1603077369261981696][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6605513,38.0876815,11z][Bakhmutske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6969475,38.0538431,11z][Soledar]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4682884,37.9557667,11z][Kurdyumivka]]
- Around Donetsk, Russia [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1603077406813667328][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0572476,37.5736284,14z][Nevelske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9147295,37.4588834,11z][Pobjeda]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.8534122,37.4742253,11z][Novomykhailivka]]
- According to Pentagon officials, Iran has [[https://www.washingtonpost.com/national-security/2022/12/09/russia-iran-drone-missile/?outputType=amp][agreed to supply 6000 aircraft]], mostly Shahed loitering munitions, to Russia
  - Iran also agreed to set up a UAV factory in Russia's Tartarstan region
  - In exchange Russia may also agree to supply Iran with its S-400 air defense system, in addition to the reported Su-35 deliveries
- The US is reportedly [[https://www.washingtonpost.com/national-security/2022/12/14/ukraine-smart-bomb-jdams/][planning to send]] Ukraine JDAM conversion kits to turn Ukraine's unguided bombs into precision weapons
  - /But how effective will these kits be, given that Ukrainian planes can't drop from medium or high altitudes?/
- A Reuters investigation on how Russia [[https://www.reuters.com/investigates/special-report/ukraine-crisis-russia-tech-middlemen/][smuggles dual-use components]] for its weapons industry
  - Multiple cutouts
  - Often use Turkish firms which have German proxies
  - Another route is via Hong Kong
- Apparently Russian forces are [[https://twitter.com/wartranslated/status/1602955036304220161][attacking with smaller groups of infantry]]
  - Smaller groups are easier to manage and motivate
  - However, this means that casualties are higher

** 2022-12-13 Tuesday
- Near Svatove, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1602740595436683264][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.5222553,37.9480571,13z][Novoselivske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.4794448,37.889303,11z][Stelmakhivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.3292539,37.9405371,13z][Novojehorivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.2200192,37.9465744,11z][Makiivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1314083,38.1373012,11z][Chervonopopivka]]
- Near Siversk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1602740600578736135][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271478,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8603853,38.1878152,11z][Verkhnokamyanske]]
- Near Bakhmut, Russian forces [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1602740606165520386][attacked]] ([[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1602740617343385601][2]]) [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7145913,38.1364423,11z][Yakolivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6969475,38.0538431,11z][Soledar]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6605513,38.0876815,11z][Bakhmutske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4682884,37.9557667,11z][Kurdyumivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.5279761,37.9495319,11z][Klishchiivka]]
  - Yakolivka, Bakhmutske, and Kurdyumivka have all been reported as captured by Russian sources, but fighting is ongoing there
- Near Donetsk, Russia [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1602740624087973888][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.1451452,37.727358,11z][Avdiivka]]
- More intense than usual shelling [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1602740631440429057][reported]] in Zaporizhzhia, but the reason is unclear
- Russian soldiers are [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1602809815872462849][fighting in 50-year-old body armor]]
- Apparently Russian soldiers [[https://twitter.com/Tatarigami_UA/status/1602463040292753408][believe they're fighting Poles]] in Ukraine
  - /Seems like they're taking Russian propaganda about this being a war against NATO literally/
- The explosion in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@52.7552727,32.2312885,11z][Klintsy]], Bryansk Oblast, was reportedly the result of a [[https://twitter.com/Osinttechnical/status/1602593461294833666][strike with a Tochka ballistic missile]]
- The US Department of Justice [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1602764716346155010][indicted 7 people]] for attempting to smuggle sniper rifle ammunition and sensitive technology to Russia
- The Biden Administration is reportedly [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1602716394034008065][finalizing plans to send Patriot air-defense systems to Ukraine]]
  - /Let's wait until the plans are actually finalized and officially announced before reacting/
- According to the Estonian Defense Forces, Russia has [[https://news.err.ee/1608815692/edf-intelligence-chief-russia-still-has-long-term-offensive-capabilities][enough ammunition]] for its heavy weapons to last through 2023
  - /Russia had huge reserves of Soviet-era weapons and ammunition, and while they may not be the best and most modern systems, they're still functional/
- Ukraine is [[https://www.ft.com/content/fbd6dc6e-4a41-4bfa-977b-8c3ef4482dcc][burning through its stocks of anti-aircraft weapons]] at a rapid rate
- Great Britain [[https://www.gov.uk/government/news/pm-announces-new-air-defence-for-ukraine-on-first-visit-to-kyiv][supplies more anti-aircraft weapons]] to Ukraine
- Ukrainian mud is [[https://twitter.com/Osinttechnical/status/1602776148731396096][something else]]
  - /Highlights the need for Ukraine to receive tracked armored vehicles/
  - /Wheeled vehicles, such as HIMARS, can move more rapidly on paved roads or hard-packed soil, but they'll quickly bog down in this kind of mud/
- Russian TV [[https://twitter.com/wartranslated/status/1602725530691936256][airs a segment]] where a Russian soldier captured as a POW in Ukraine says that he was treated well and the Geneva Conventions were followed

** 2022-12-12 Monday
- Near Svatove, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1602381500233748482][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.4794448,37.889303,11z][Stelmakhivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.2200192,37.9465744,11z][Makiivka]]
- Near Kreminna, Russian forces [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1602381506483191823][attacked]] Ukrainian troops in the Serebryanka Forestry Area, north of the Siversky Donetsk river from [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9411955,38.1537086,11z][Serebryanka]]
- [[https://twitter.com/wartranslated/status/1602395299145711648][Footage]] of the liberation of [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.6420886,37.8921433,11z][Kyslivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.6298994,37.9021945,11z][Kotlyarivka]], which were recaptured by Ukraine around 2022-12-08
- Near Bakhmut, Ukrainian sources [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1602381512510431234][report]] Russian attacks on [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7329344,38.2110851,11z][Bilohorivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6969475,38.0538431,11z][Soledar]], while Russian sources also report that they attacked [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6354395,38.0192917,11z][Pidhorodne]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.5010055,37.9621283,14z][Andriivka]]
- Donetsk
  - Russia [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1602381518235746306][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.3137765,37.8303974,11z][Yuryivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0095154,37.467888,11z][Krasnohorivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]]
  - Heavy fighting was also [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1602381523839221772][reported]] near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.1451452,37.727358,11z][Avdiivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.1729265,37.7814818,11z][Kamyanka]]
- Russia also [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1602381529585418241][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.8406869,36.8208355,11z][Velyka Novosilka]] for the second day in a row
- Russian sources are claiming that Ukrainian saboteurs [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1602420073557524480][damaged a bridge]] in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@46.8434099,35.3212658,11z][Melitopol]]
- Explosions [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1602429240837902336][were reported]] in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@52.7552727,32.2312885,11z][Klintsy]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@52.3816909,32.1669961,11z][Klimovo]], Bryansk Oblast, Russia
- There was an [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1602350002348720132][assassination attempt]] on the the deputy head of the occupation authority of Kherson Oblast, Vitaliy Bulyuk
  - Car was blown up
  - Driver was killed
  - Bulyuk was taken to the hospital in serious condition
- Iran will reportedly [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1602349277321334788][limit the range of the missiles]] it ships to Russia, in an effort to avoid further sanctions
- The Russians are [[https://twitter.com/KofmanMichael/status/1602211739319566337][expending huge amounts of resources]] in Bakhmut, for only tactical gains
  - Expenditure of artillery ammunition may prove to be especially significnt
  - May compromise Russia's ability to defend elsewhere
- [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1602272177868390400][TOS-1A strike]] on [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.5222553,37.9480571,13z][Novoselivske]]
  - /Not sure what the purpose of that was/
  - /Given how shattered the buildings are, any likely Ukrainian forces are probably either in trenches or underground, neither of which are particularly vulnerable to thermobaric munitions/
- The UK Minister of Defense, Ben Wallace, is [[https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/uk-minister-is-open-minded-over-sending-longer-range-weapons-ukraine-2022-12-12/][open to supplying Ukraine with longer ranged weapons]] if Russia keeps hitting Ukrainian civilian infrastructure
- Mobilized Russians are [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1602409553362096129][falling ill with respiratory ailments]] at training camps in Siberia, where they are reportedly being housed in tents during sub-zero weather
  - Tents are being heated by wood-burning stoves
  - Soldiers are having to buy their own medicine or have it delivered by relatives
- The fire in the barracks in Crimea (see 2022-12-10) was reportedly [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1602236699505221632][caused by the misuse of a potbellied stove]] for heating


** 2022-12-11 Sunday
- Near Kupyansk, Ukraine has continuing to struggle to expand its bridgehead across the Oskil River by [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1601932550942982144][attacking]] towards [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.5831775,38.1514004,11z][Nyzhnia Duvanka]]
- Near Svatove, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1601932557863587843][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.4246428,37.9013316,12z][Andriivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.5222553,37.9480571,13z][Novoselivske]], in an attempt to push Ukrainian forces back from the P66 highway
- Near Kreminna, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1601932571528646656][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1314083,38.1373012,11z][Chervonopopivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.0974123,38.1786402,11z][Zhytlivka]]
  - Russian sources also [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1601932571528646656][report]] a Russian counterattack near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1669387,37.9575929,11z][Nevske]]
  - The fact that a Russian attack was reported on Zhytlivka [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1601932601568251904][seems to indicate]] that Ukrainian forces are closing on Kreminna
- Near Siversk, Russia [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1601932571528646656][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271478,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9411955,38.1537086,11z][Serebryanka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8603853,38.1878152,11z][Verkhnokamyanske]]
- /No news out of Bakhmut or Donetsk today/
- There was possibly an [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1601955178080600064][attack]] near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.8406869,36.8208355,11z][Velyka Novosilka]], but details are sketchy
  - [[https://twitter.com/Osinttechnical/status/1602078347877617664][Footage]] of the failed Russian attack near Velyka Novosilka
- [[https://twitter.com/NOELreports/status/1601877278425767937][Proof]] that Bakhmut is still under Ukrainian control
- The Ukrainian Minister of Defense, Oleksii Reznikov, admits that the wheeled vehicles that Ukraine is predominantly using [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1602082523206635521][struggle with the mud, slush and snow of the Ukrainian winter]]
- Russian commentators are [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1602064765123174403][bemoaning the lack of UAVs in the Russian army]] --- say that Russian artillery is blind due to a lack of UAVs for spotting
- A Russian Su-24 that was lost near Bakhmut was reportedly [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1602056976187498496][being flown by a Wagner pilot]] on behalf of a Wagner ground commander who was calling for air support
- Lack of equipment for mobilized units is [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1602040078343225349][being blamed on regional inadequacies]]
  - /Good tsar, bad boyar/
- [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1601995113227509760][Rare footage]] of tank-versus-tank combat from [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.5222553,37.9480571,13z][Novselivske]] as a Ukrainian T-64 engages and destroys a Russian T-72
- Also out of Novoselivske, a Ukrainian drone [[https://twitter.com/bayraktar_1love/status/1601942469024825344][blows up a pile of Russian ammunition]]
- The strike in Melitopol yesterday was apparently on a [[https://twitter.com/IntelCrab/status/1601697039452364800][spa/resort that had been converted into a barracks for Russian troops]]
- Russian soldiers are likely [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1602028477007413250][fighting on reduced calories]] in some cases
- A Russian reporter [[https://twitter.com/fdov21/status/1601374679431725057][gives away the positions of Russian artillery]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.611512,38.144834,11z][near Bakhmut]]

** 2022-12-10 Saturday
- Near Kupyansk, Russian forces are [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1601637237095280640][posing a challenge]] near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.7835617,37.7791884,11z][Vilshana]], making it difficult for Ukrainians to advance
- Near Kreminna, Russian troops [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1601637244166889472][attacked]] towards [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1669387,37.9575929,11z][Nevske]]
  - Shelling was also reported near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1314083,38.1373012,11z][Chervonopopivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1224694,38.171178,12z][Pishchane]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.995738,38.098652,11z][Dibrova]], indicating possible Ukrainian offensives
- Near Bakhmut, Russia attacked ([[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1601637251360096257][1]], [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1601637258360410112][2]]) [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7145913,38.1364423,11z][Yakolivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6969475,38.0538431,11z][Soledar]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6475906,37.9831003,12z][Pidhorodne]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.554042,38.012325,11z][Opytne]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4682884,37.9557667,11z][Kurdyumivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4104667,37.9059626,11z][Druzhba]]
  - /Def Mon is is downplaying Russian success around Yakolivka, but it seems to me that Russia has made some progress here/
- Near Donetsk, Russia [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1601637265301991424][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0572476,37.5736284,14z][Nevelske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9147295,37.4588834,11z][Pobjeda]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.8534122,37.4742253,11z][Novomykhailivka]]
- [[https://twitter.com/vcdgf555/status/1601661482181464064][Multiple HIMARS explosions]] reported in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@46.8434099,35.3212658,11z][Melitopol]]
- Video of a [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1601664785594351616][new Russian loitering munition]]
  - Designed to be cheap
  - 1kg warhead
  - /Unclear how effective this will be against armored targets with such a small warhead/
- Many of the self-propelled artillery pieces sent to Ukraine by NATO countries are [[https://www.wsj.com/articles/many-of-ukraines-western-weapons-await-repairs-far-from-the-front-line-11670667085][not available due to maintenance requirements]]
  - Less than 50% of the PzH 2000s that Germany has sent Ukraine are available for combat because they must be Lithuania for maintenance
  - Servicing of Ukrainian weapons is hampered by tension between Germany and Poland
  - Poland insists that its own firms carry out repairs with the aid of confidential technical information that Germany is unwilling to supply
  - Poland does not impose this requirement on the UK or the United States
  - As a result, Germany is turning to Slovakia to set up a new repair center for Ukrainian weapons
  - Ukraine lacks the spare parts, workshops and tooling to carry out repairs on Western equipment
- US officials state that [[https://www.thedrive.com/the-war-zone/pilot-training-indicates-russia-will-deliver-su-35s-to-iran-next-year][Iran will be receiving Su-35 fighter aircraft]] as of next year
  - Iran will reportedly be giving Russia hundreds of short range ballistic missiles in exchange
  - The fighters that Iran will be receiving were originally intended for Egypt
  - However, Egypt canceled its order under the threat of US secondary sanctions last year
  - /This means that Iran will have more advanced fighter aircraft than India/
- The Pentagon has given Ukraine a [[https://www.thetimes.co.uk/article/ukraine-drone-warfare-russia-732jsshpx][tacit endorsement]] to carry out strikes inside Russia
  - US officials are reportedly less concerned now about the escalatory potential of these strikes
  - However the US is still wary of publicly endorsing or encouraging these attacks
  - Ukraine has been careful to use only its own weapons for these attacks
  - More US advisors are suggesting that the US should supply Ukraine with longer-range higher-endurance Gray Eagle UAVs and longer range ATACMS missiles
- Ukrainian road crews are working to [[https://twitter.com/Osinttechnical/status/1601368721934938113][repair the road]] into Kherson city
- Morocco will [[https://twitter.com/WarInUkraineYet/status/1601590726877335552][provide Ukraine with spare parts for its T-72s]]
- A [[https://twitter.com/WarInUkraineYet/status/1601576856712794115][large fire has been reported]] in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@44.5313206,34.1836161,11z][Sovjetske, Crimea]], in a building housing Russian soldiers
- The Russian authorities are reportedly [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1601670888013062144][deceitfully recruiting immigrants]] from Central Asia
  - Immigrants are being enticed with promises of Russian citizenship
  - However, legally, foreigners are not allowed to serve in the Russian military
  - In addition, many of the countries that these immigrants hail from prohibit their citizens from serving in foreign militaries
  - However, none of this is stopping in immigration centers from offering military service contracts to immigrants
  - Migrants from Central Asia have been captured by Ukrainian forces, so it is clear that some of them are getting into combat
  - Beyond that, it's unclear how these immigrants are being used by the Russian military
  - /My theory is that this is less a large conspiracy and more a result of low-level corruption/
  - /Regions have quotas on how many conscripts they need to supply/
  - /Getting immigrants into the recruitment pipeline allows provincial officials to recruit fewer Russian citizens, which reduces political backlash/
- Narendra Modi [[https://www.reuters.com/world/india-pm-modi-skip-annual-summit-with-russias-putin-et-now-2022-12-09/][cancels a bilateral summit]] with Vladimir Putin

** 2022-12-09 Friday
- Near Kreminna, Russian forces [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1601297210116780032][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271478,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1314083,38.1373012,11z][Chervonopopivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.2061799,38.0825557,11z][Ploshchanka]]
  - /The status of Ploshchanka is still unclear to me/
- Near Bakhmut, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1601297216773103618][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.5279761,37.9495319,11z][Klishchiivka]]
- Near Donetsk, Russian forces [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1601297223312379904][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]], and possibly lost some ground in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0683512,37.6972295,11z][Pisky]]
  - /Looks like Pisky is contested once again --- Russian forces have been pushed back from the town, but it doesn't look like Ukrainian forces have re-established positions within the town/
- Dara Massicot has a good [[https://twitter.com/MassDara/status/1601206587485745155][thread]] on the adjustments the Russian military is making as it transitions to the defensive
  - It appears, from Putin's public statements, that Russian's new commander Surovikin is comfortable sharing honest assessments of the war
  - Surovikin appears to be the most competent Russian commander thus far
  - Organized an orderly retreat from Kherson
  - Better prepared defenses
  - Increased strikes against Ukrainian infrastructure to stretch and deplete Ukrainian air defenses
- Financial Times [[https://www.ft.com/content/dcdd09bf-440a-4648-9664-6084b11dddd4][article]] on the battle near Bakhmut
  - Bakhmut is a meatgrinder for the Russians
  - World War 1 style infatry charges into fixed positions
  - Both sides are taking casualties but are not saying how many
  - Russian troops have a foothold on the easter edge of the city, but have been unable to advance further
  - Both sides are moving reinforcements from other regions to Bakhmut
- Satellite analysis shows [[https://twitter.com/konrad_muzyka/status/1601189324418330624][fewer Russian tanks in Belarus]]
- [[https://twitter.com/WarInUkraineYet/status/1601269050772160513][More shelling]] in central [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.011805,37.8006582,11z][Donetsk]]
- Putin engages in more [[https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2022-12-09/putin-says-russia-may-add-nuclear-first-strike-to-strategy][nuclear saber rattling]]
  - Talks about formally adding nuclear first strikes as an option in Russian policy
  - Is reportedly a response to the US's "prompt global strike" concept, which envisions a capacity to hit any target anywhere with a precision weapon within one hour
- Transport trucks loaded with dragon's teeth [[https://twitter.com/neonhandrail/status/1601057256690585600][spotted heading west]] in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.525701,39.111197,11z][Vesela Tarasivka]], Luhansk Oblast
- Putin [[https://twitter.com/wartranslated/status/1601285543094276097][admits the war may go on for a long time]]
- A Russian soldier [[https://twitter.com/wartranslated/status/1601205507355660290][claims]] that Russia is using tanks as makeshift indirect fire because it doesn't have enough ammunition for its howitzers
- [[https://twitter.com/Osinttechnical/status/1601104230982770688][Drifting Humvee]] on Ukrainian ice

** 2022-12-08 Thursday
- Near Svatove, Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1600926849672302592][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.4794448,37.889303,11z][Stelmakhivka]]
  - Ukraine has liberated [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.6420886,37.8921433,11z][Kyslivka]]
    - /Last news from Kyslivka was from 2022-11-01, when Ukrainians and Russians were contesting the town/
    - /It appears that Russian forces have retreated from the area/
  - Ukrainian forces also appear to have made progress near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.6565534,37.8594326,12z][Stepova Novoselivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.6298994,37.9021945,11z][Kotlyarivka]], but neither of those villages can be considered liberated yet
  - /Still making progress towards [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.6599919,37.9266782,11z][Yahidne]]/
- Near Kreminna, Russia attacked [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.2061799,38.0825557,11z][Ploshchanka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1314083,38.1373012,11z][Chervonopopivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271478,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]]
- Near Bakhmut, Russia attacked ([[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1600926880235806720][1]]) ([[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1600926887228100609][2]]) [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7634233,38.2371188,11z][Berestove]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7329344,38.2110851,11z][Bilohorivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7145913,38.1364423,11z][Yakolivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6605513,38.0876815,11z][Bakhmutske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.554042,38.012325,11z][Opytne]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4682884,37.9557667,11z][Kurdyumivka]]
  - The situation around Yakolivka is unclear --- Russian sources are saying that the town is captured, but Ukrainian forces and satellite data indicate that the town is still contested
  - The same applies to Kurdyumivka --- it's clear that there's still fighting going on there, even though Russian forces say they have captured the town
  - /This is similar to the situation in Pisky, where Russia claimed that the town was captured in August, but the town wasn't actually captured until October/
  - /Another analogous situation is Soledar, where some Russian soldiers took a selfie in a factory at the south end of the town and claimed that the entire town had been captured/
- Near Donetsk, Russian forces [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1600926894391975936][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.8534122,37.4742253,11z][Novomykhailivka]]
- Russian sources are [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1600926902566297605][reporting Ukrainian activity]] on [[https://www.google.com/maps/@46.5555524,32.5065058,12z][Bilohrudove Island]] in the Dnipro delta, however it's unclear whether this is just raiding activity or whether the Ukrainians are trying to make a concerted push to permanently occupy the island
- A Russian ammunition depot in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@46.3645012,33.5164761,11z][Chaplynka]], Kherson Oblast, [[https://twitter.com/bayraktar_1love/status/1600798365859876864][blew up]]
- Ukrainian soldiers [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1600909630846242820][use a counter-UAV gun]] to capture a Russian quadcopter
- The Russian Deputy Minister of Defense [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1600874586325024771][visited Tehran]] recently
- The US [[https://twitter.com/NatashaBertrand/status/1600838999119392769][completed the exchange]] of Viktor Bout for Brittney Griner
- Ukrainians [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1600921614266544128][mount helicopter rocket pods on a command post vehicle]] and use it as a makeshift MLRS
- Germany will [[https://twitter.com/ukraine_map/status/1600703274814144513][sell Ukraine 18 RCH-155 self-propelled howitzers]]
  - /Looks like a very capable howitzer --- only needs a crew of two, and has a fire rate of 30 rounds per minute/
  - However, deliveries [[https://en.defence-ua.com/news/ukraine_can_to_buy_german_rch_155_self_propelled_howitzers-4251.html][won't begin until 2025]]
- Turkey is [[https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2022-12-08/turkey-plans-talks-with-russia-to-seek-discount-on-gas-imports-lberqt7r][seeking a 25% discount]] on Russian natural gas
  - Turkey wants the discount to apply *retroactively*, covering payments made in 2022 and 2023
  - Apparently Hungary has a 6-month payment deferral for Russian gas
- A Ukrainian pilot managed to [[https://www.forbes.com/sites/davidaxe/2022/12/08/his-mig-29-in-flames-blood-pouring-down-his-face-this-ukrainian-pilot-still-managed-to-snap-a-selfie/?sh=4cef767157c9][snap a selfie of himself]] after ejecting from his plane after it was brought down by an exploding drone
  - /Taking "do it for the 'gram" to a whole new level/
- Russia is reportedly [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1600902119552438272][recruiting more prisoners]]
  - Recruitment is being conducted by the Russian government this time, not Wagner
  - Government officials are being scrupulous about ensuring that they record the prisoners volunteering to serve --- apparently they are afraid of blowback from wives and mothers if it appears as if prisoners are being conscripted
- A pro-Russia Telegram channel admits that the [[https://twitter.com/wartranslated/status/1600937673304469504][equipping and provisioning of mobilized units has been uneven]]
  - Admits that there have been some cases of soldiers freezing to death
  - Says that "companies" have been lost to pneumonia
  - Insists, however, that the majority of mobilized troops are well equipped and provisioned

** 2022-12-07 Wednesday
- Near Svatove, it's possible that the Ukrainians have [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1600580476778987533][pushed the Russians further back]] near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.5222553,37.9480571,13z][Novoselivske]]
- Near Siversk, Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1600580482873311250][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271337,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8603853,38.1878152,11z][Verkhnokamyanske]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8075094,38.2507431,11z][Spirne]]
- Near Bakhmut, Russian forces [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1600580488510455820][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7145913,38.1364423,11z][Yakolivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4682884,37.9557667,11z][Kurdyumivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4820179,37.8600578,12z][Bila Hora]]
  - The Bila Hora attack is strange because Bila Hora is to the west of Kurdyumivka
  - It's possible that the Russians have captured Kurdyumivka, but that doesn't make sense given the reports by the Ukrainians of ongoing fighting in the city
  - Another possibility is that Russian forces are attacking northward from near the [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.3808905,37.9314599,11z][Shumy]]/[[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.3921847,37.9034419,12z][Pivnichne]] area
  - /I think the only firm conclusion that can be drawn is the one that has been obvious for months/
  - /Russia is unable to attack Bakhmut directly, so they're launching repeated attacks to its north and south in order to try to encircle the city/
- Near Donetsk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1600580501210808345][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.2489705,37.7731833,11z][Novobakhmutivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0095154,37.467888,11z][Krasnohorivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.8534122,37.4742253,11z][Novomykhailivka]]
- [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1600610004075159563][Large fires]] reported near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.1451452,37.727358,11z][Avdiivka]], reportedly as a result of Russian incendiary munitions
- Aid to Ukraine is reportedly [[https://asia.nikkei.com/Politics/Ukraine-war/Germany-struggles-to-get-China-parts-to-replenish-ammo-stockpile][depleting German ammunition stockpiles]]
  - Germany is facing bottlenecks in procuring
    - Ammunition
    - Special steels
    - Cotton linters for manufacturing the bags that hold propellant charges
  - German ammunition manufacturers are also complaining about the German government's reluctance to commit to additional funding and long-term contracts
- President Putin says [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1600501052960378883][no further mobilization necessary at this time]]
  - Says that only 150,000 of the 300,000 mobilized troops have been sent to Ukraine
  - Denies reports of mass desertions
  - Says that war is taking longer than expected
  - Highlights the encirclement of the Sea of Azov as a concrete accomplishment of the war thus far

** 2022-12-06 Tuesday
- Near Kreminna, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1600208324082794496][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271337,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]], and Russian sources are reporting Ukrainian offensives near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1224694,38.171178,12z][Pishchane]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1314083,38.1373012,11z][Chervonopopivka]]
- Near Bakhmut, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1600208330546630656][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6969475,38.0538431,11z][Soledar]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6605513,38.0876815,11z][Bakhmutske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.5010055,37.9621283,14z][Andriivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4682884,37.9557667,11z][Kurdyumivka]]; Russian sources also reported fighting in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.554042,38.012325,11z][Opytne]]
- Near Donetsk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1600208337462697984][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0095154,37.467888,11z][Krasnohorivka]] (/I went with the southern one because it seems like that's the one that the Russians attacked most recently/)
  - /Donetsk has gotten quieter over the past few days/
- Ukraine [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1600098463496085506][attacked]] a third airfield in Russian territory, [[https://www.google.com/maps/@51.7509965,36.3015055,8080m/data=!3m1!1e3][near Kursk]]
- In addition to the airfield, Ukrainians also [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1600068201756254209][attacked]] fuel infrastructure in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@52.964384,32.407546,15z][Lesnoe]], Bryansk Oblast, Russia
  - This fuel depot was attacked previously on 2022-11-30
  - The reason it didn't catch fire this time is because the tanks that were hit happened to be empty
- The US [[https://www.defensenews.com/pentagon/2022/12/05/army-plans-dramatic-ammo-production-boost-as-ukraine-drains-stocks/][announces more details]] on increased artillery ammunition production
  - Goal is to have a capacity of 40,000 shells per month
  - Army is planning to increase production at three factories
  - Will also work with foreign partners to increase their production
- Apparently some of the cruise missiles that struck Ukraine in the latest wave of attacks were [[https://www.nytimes.com/2022/12/05/us/politics/cruise-missiles-russia-ukraine-sanctions.html][manufactured after sanctions had been imposed]]
  - /Shouldn't find this too surprising/
  - /Sanctions always take longer than expected to have an effect/
  - /All it tells us is that Russia has enough parts in stock (or is able to scrounge enough parts from other domestic sources​/smuggling to maintain a limited rate of production)/
- President Zelensky [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1600080485568290816][visits Slovyansk]]
- Russian [[https://twitter.com/Osinttechnical/status/1599939421658574848][loitering munition strikes]] against Ukrainian air defense assets
  - /Footage seems to come from earlier in the year, given the fact that the grass is green/
  - /Interesting to see that the Russian propaganda includes a number of instances where the loitering munition appears to miss the target/
- Poland accepts a German Patriot air defense system, but [[https://apnews.com/article/nato-europe-poland-mariusz-blaszczak-government-and-politics-89fea9e31e1c0b229e4e96eaa42bbec2][argues that it would have been better placed in Western Ukraine]]
- Hungary [[https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/eu-looks-win-hungary-support-ukraine-aid-return-eu-funds-access-2022-12-06/][vetoes]] an €18 billion aid package for Ukraine
  - This is speculated to be retaliation for the EU blocking funds to Hungary over concerns about corruption and democratic norms
- A [[https://twitter.com/neonhandrail/status/1600072852598030336][convoy]] of T-90M tanks spotted in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.2775917,38.9066081,11z][Starobilsk]], Luhansk
- Reporting from inside Russia suggests that mobilized troops are [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1600049390520913920][largely dependent on civilian-provided aid packages]] for their basic needs
  - Reports also indicate that mobilized units in Ukraine are picking and cooking unharvested corn
  - /One thing to note is that whenever I see these reports, it's always in the context of some unit from some random ethnic republic in the middle of nowhere, Siberia/
  - /My read is that the outfitting and provisioning of mobilized units was left up to the provincial governments (rather like how it was with the early Union army in the Civil War)/
  - /Given the drastic levels of wealth inequality between provinces in Russia, this has led to large differences in the quality and quantity of supplies provided to mobilized Russian troops in Ukraine/
- Igor Girkin [[https://twitter.com/wartranslated/status/1600112329059958786][once again criticizes]] the Russian government for not having a clear strategic goal in Ukraine
  - Says that most units have no idea what they're doing in Ukraine
  - Draws a contrast between "apathetic" regular Russian Army units and his own supposedly more motivated Donetsk and Luhansk People's Republic militias
  - /Going by battlefield results and external reporting, however, it's difficult to draw any kind of distinction between the performance of the regular Russian army and the Donetsk and Luhansk People's Republic militias/
  - /This is likely Girkin trying to make himself look good by comparison/

- Near Svatove

- Near Siversk, more [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1599092701965656064][airstrikes were reported]] near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8603712,38.1878152,11z][Verkhnokamyanka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8075094,38.2507431,11z][Spirne]], but no ground assaults
- Near Bakhmut, Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1599092709150445568][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6969475,38.0538431,11z][Soledar]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.554042,38.012325,11z][Opytne]]
- Near Donetsk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1599092725713752064][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0572476,37.5736284,14z][Nevelske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0095154,37.467888,11z][Krasnohorivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]]
- [[https://twitter.com/Tatarigami_UA/status/1599074248647057408][Thread]] on the Russian build-up near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.7790919,37.2438917,11z][Vuhledar]], and why that area is so significant
  - Russian logistics are heavily rail-dependent
  - Russian forces are probably working to secure an alternate rail line to their forces in Ukraine, because of damage to the Kerch Bridge
  - Vuhledar, Novomykhailivka and Marinka are all locations from which Ukrainian artillery can shell the railway
  - Vuhledar is especially important, because artillery positioned there can also shell [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.5979366,37.4660035,11z][Volnovakha]], a town that the Russians are using as a supply hub
    - /Volnovakha was captured by Russia some time around 2022-03-14/
  - Intense Russian attacks were able to push Ukrainians out of the town just south of Vuhledar, [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.7544122,37.2092803,11z][Pavlivka]], at great cost
    - /Pavlivka was captured by Russia early in the war, not sure when/
    - /It was liberated by Ukraine some time around 2022-06-23/
    - /Ukrainians reportedly retreated from Pavlivka on 2022-11-19/
  - However, the Ukrainian presence in Vuhledar has prevented Russian forces from advancing into Pavlivka, turning the town into a no-man's-land
  - It seems like Russian commanders will try another big assault to retake Vuhledar
- The Russian Minister of Defense, Sergei Shoigu, [[https://twitter.com/konrad_muzyka/status/1599169936961568768][has arrived in Belarus]] for talks with his Belarussian counterpart, Viktor Khrenin
  - Visit was unannounced
  - Shoigu and Khrenin reportedly signed amendments to the treaty establishing the Union State alliance between Russia and Belarus
  - Changes pertained to defense and security cooperation between the two countries
  - /Not sure why Shoigu and Khrenin are the ones signing this; I'd have thought that changes to a treaty would required signatures from heads of government, i.e. Putin and Lukashenko/
  - After meeting with Khrenin, Shoigu met with Lukashenko
  - The changes to the treaty might be legal preparation for subordinating the Belarussian military to the Western Military District in Russia
  - Konrad Muzyka's assessment is that too much is going on for this to be a diversionary operation aimed at keeping Ukrainian forces fixed near Kyiv
  - He expects more direct Belarussian involvement in the war over the coming weeks, but it's not certain what form that involvement will take
- Russian forces are [[https://twitter.com/neonhandrail/status/1598897947659636736][working on defensive fortifications]] near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.286749,35.529709,11z][Kokhane]], Zaporizhzhia Oblast
- [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1599118893272137729][Thread]] on the effects of winter weather on Russian soldiers
  - It seems that a significant number of Russian soldiers are dying of hypothermia in the field
  - Russian commanders are deliberately misreporting causes of death in order to try to obscure this fact
- The mobilization of utility workers is reportedly [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1599043912861106176][causing outages of heat and electricity]] in Russia itself
- More [[https://twitter.com/Osinttechnical/status/1599154803870834688][crazy Ukrainian helicopter flying]]
- A [[https://zona.media/article/2022/12/01/mariupol][diary of a Russian contruction worker]] in Mariupol (use Google Translate)

- Near Donetsk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1598754726593568768][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.087187,37.5934123,11z][Pervomaiske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0095154,37.467888,11z][Krasnohorivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]]
- [[https://twitter.com/moklasen/status/1598811221603471360][Video]] of fighting near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.07,37.647,11z][Pervomaiske]]
- [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1598754707492708352][Video]] of fighting in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6969475,38.0538431,11z][Soledar]]
- The Financial Times has [[https://www.ft.com/content/a781fb71-49bb-4052-ab05-a87386bf3d5e][an article]] on how the Ukraine War has exposed shortcomings in NATO's preparation of high intensity conventional conflict
  - The need to supply Ukraine while maintaining adequate stockpiles at home has exposed weaknesses in US production capacity, especially for systems like Javelins and Stingers
  - The UK has had to turn to a "third party" to replenish its stocks of NLAWs
  - France could only supply CAESAR self-propelled artillery systems to Ukraine by diverting a shipment that was originally intended for Denmark
  - There are two reasons for this inventory depletion
    - Countries have reaped a peace dividend after the end of the Cold War by limiting investments in military capacity
      - Switched to "just-in-time" manufacturing and lower inventories to reduce cost
      - These practices were adequate for lower-intensity counterinsurgencies, but may not be adequate for high-intensity conventional warfare
      - The British Army's existing stockpile of artillery ammunition is equivalent to only two days of Russian usage or one week of Ukrainian usage
    - There is ongoing budget uncertainty
      - European governments have not allocated additional money to rearmament, despite saying that rearmament is necessary
      - No defense contractor is willing to build additional capacity without some kind of assurance that customers will be available
      - Countries have not streamlined or sped up their procurement processes
      - Current procedures are oriented towards topping up inventories only after they've been depleted by conflict, rather than procuring weapons ahead of time
      - This creates a very "choppy" demand signal that discourages investment in additional capacity
  - /I see clear parallels between the bureaucratic failures during the pandemic and the bureaucratic failures during the Ukraine War/
  - /In both instances, Western governments are failing to acknowledge that risk​/reward ratios have shifted and it might be okay to pay more in order to have immediate delivery/
  - /For example, look at how the European governments wasted months negotiating with pharmaceutical companies over single-digit percentage discounts for COVID vaccines while their economies were under lockdown and the pandemic was raging/
- A fuel depot in the city of [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0624995,38.4180699,11z][Shakhtarsk, Donetsk]] has [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1598717330909204480][caught fire]]
  - /Shakhtarsk is within HIMARS range of the front line, but it's unclear whether this was the result of a HIMARS strike, sabotage, or an accident/
- The G7 [[https://www.reuters.com/business/energy/holdout-poland-approves-eus-60-russian-oil-price-cap-with-adjustment-mechanism-2022-12-02/][agrees to a $60/barrel price cap]] on the Russian crude oil
  - Applies to seaborne crude
  - Price cap agreed to by the G7 + Australia
  - Price will be $60/barrel or 5% below market rate, whichever is lower
  - Goal is to hurt Russian revenues while limiting the damage to global energy markets
- The Russian republic of Buryatia is sending [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1598686609892859905][magic yurts]] to protect soldiers from HIMARS strikes
  - /It's easy to laugh at this, but it [[https://samzdat.com/2017/06/19/the-use-and-abuse-of-witchdoctors-for-life/][might be effective]] at keeping Russian soldiers from panicking/
- According to Russian sources, [[https://twitter.com/wartranslated/status/1598666470556327942][non-essential personnel are being evacuated]] from [[https://www.google.com/maps/@46.7506705,33.343781,11z][Nova Kakhovka]]
- Germany will be [[https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/germany-send-seven-additional-gepard-tanks-ukraine-spiegel-2022-12-02/][sending another 7 Gepard anti-aircraft]] systems to Ukraine
- Finland [[https://valtioneuvosto.fi/en/-//1410869/finland-supports-energy-sector-in-ukraine][sends electrical grid components]] to Ukraine
  - Transformers, circuit breakers and relays to replace equipment damaged by Russian airstrikes
  - Generators and heating equipment to supplement the electrical grid
  - Aid will be sent via the EU civil protection mechanism

  - There are reports that Russian forces have advanced into Kurdyumivka, but it appears that the town is still contested

- Russian MiG-31s, capable of carrying the hypersonic Kinzhal missile, are [[https://twitter.com/MotolkoHelp/status/1598307262283616259][reportedly leaving Belarus]] and returning to Russia
- The US is considering [[https://www.cnn.com/2022/11/30/politics/us-military-expanding-training-ukraine][increasing the number of Ukrainians it trains at once]]
  - More intense and comprehensive training than what Ukrainians get in Poland or the UK
  - Focused on combined arms, specifically on infantry/artillery coordination
  - Training would reportedly take place at the US base in Grafenwoehr
  - German officials haven't officially been contacted, but indicate that they would be willing to grant the necessary approvals
- The US has commissioned a $1.2 billion contract with Raytheon to [[https://www.reuters.com/world/us/pentagon-award-12-bln-contract-raytheon-ukrainian-nasams-source-document-2022-11-30/][manufacture additional NASAMS]] systems for Ukraine
- [[https://www.nytimes.com/2022/12/01/world/europe/spain-letter-bombs.html][Letter bombs were sent]] to various Ukraine-related targets in Spain
  - Letter bombs were mailed to the office of the Prime Minister, the office of the Defense Minister, a Spanish defense contractor, the European Union Satellite Center, the Ukrainian embassy and the US embassy
  - The only bomb that went off was the one that went to the Ukrainian embassy, which caused minor injuries to the person opening the package
  - All other bombs were intercepted by law enforcement and disposed of by bomb squads
  - No demands or explanations have been given
- The Wagner Group has reportedly [[https://is.gd/TQllKb][created a "Wild Company"]] consisting of its most violent convicts
  - Revives practice used in prior wars, going back to World War 1 and the Russian Civil War
  - These companies are often known for carrying out war crimes
  - Reportedly flies a skull and crossbones flag
- A mobilized soldier [[https://is.gd/Di7qJB][reviews his sleeping quarters]]
  - /See Jack Watling's thread from 2022-11-27 for why wet sleeping aren't just uncomfortable, but rather pose a danger to combat readiness/

- Near Siversk, Russian sources report that the Russian military [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1598030075668176896][launched attacks]] on [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8603712,38.1878152,11z][Verkhnokamyanske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9411955,38.1537086,11z][Serebryanka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271337,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]]
- Bakhmut
  - Russia [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1598030081922060288][launched attacks]] on [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6605513,38.0876815,11z][Bakhmutske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7329344,38.2110851,11z][Bilohorivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7145913,38.1364423,11z][Yakolivka]]
  - Ukraine [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1598030092080451613][may have retreated]] from [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4682884,37.9557667,11z][Kurdyumikva]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4750907,37.9636501,13z][Zelenopillya]], but this is speculative
- Near Donetsk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1598030101169737728][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.087187,37.5934123,11z][Pervomaiske]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0572476,37.5736284,14z][Nevelske]]
- In Zaporizhzhia, [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1598074221284200448][more explosions reported]] in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.2489702,35.685411,11z][Tokmak]]
- Russian mobilized reserves are being [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1597933615450841089][housed in unheated tents]] as the outside temperature drops to -20°C
- [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1597904188088147968][Low flying Ukrainian Su-25 with MiG-29 escort]]
- [[https://www.economist.com/science-and-technology/2022/11/30/lessons-from-russias-cyber-war-in-ukraine][Lessons from cyberwarfare in Ukraine]]
  - Russia launched numerous cyberattacks on Ukraine in the run-up to the war
  - Some of these attacks were successful, such as the ViaSat disruption
  - However, unlike in 2014, Russia was not able to disrupt the Ukrainian electricity grid or banking infrastructure
  - This is largely due to Ukrainian efforts to harden and secure their computer networks
  - Ukraine also engaged in extensive contingency planning, which helped mitigate the damage caused by the cyberattacks that did succeed
  - Western assistance was useful
    - NATO granted Ukraine access to a library of known Russian malware
    - UK supplied firewall and forensic software
  - In exchange, Western military and intelligence officials were able to observe Russian cyberattacks on Ukraine, gaining crucial information about how Russian cyberoperations actually work
  - The relative age of Ukraine's electrical infrastructure was also an unexpected help
    - Less networked than more modern infrastructure
    - Many systems still had Soviet-era manual overrides, which Ukrainian engineers were able to operate in order to keep the grid running
  - Russian cyberattacks may have been overhyped
    - Russian attacks tend to be "loud" and more easily detected than attacks from other major world powers, such as the United States, China, or Israel
    - Tend to spill past their intended targets, giving security researchers greater opportunity to study attacks and develop countermeasures
  - The Ukraine War has exposed the limits of cyber operations
    - Not as difficult to attribute cyberattacks as initially thought
    - Requires significant time and preparation to set up successful attacks
    - Russia has not launched very many cyberattacks against NATO despite extensive NATO support for Ukraine --- might be a signal that the Russian leadership has cooled on its ardour for cyberattacks as a tool of state policy
    - Cyberattacks may be more useful in peacetime; in wartime it may be more effective to launch a missile or a drone strike
- [[https://rusi.org/explore-our-research/publications/special-resources/preliminary-lessons-conventional-warfighting-russias-invasion-ukraine-february-july-2022][RUSI report]] on the war's lessons for Western militaries
- NATO militaries [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1597996828699807744][pledge more vehicles and ammunition]] for Ukraine at the NATO summit in Bucharest
- Hungary's government [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1597931655427424259][promises to ratify]] Sweden and Finland's NATO membership in February
- The railway bridge in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.2775917,38.9066081,11z][Starobilsk]], Luhansk, [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1597864517459148802][was reportedly hit by HIMARS]]
- A fuel depot in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@52.964384,32.407546,15z][Lesnoe]], Bryansk Oblast has [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1597855112801619968][caught fire]]
  - /Unknown whether this was a genuine accident or Ukrainian sabotage/
  - /Lesnoe is approximately 100km from the Ukrainian border/
- A Russian military reporter writes that the majority of the families of mobilized troops are [[https://is.gd/ODCoba][unable to contact]] their mobilized relatives

- In Zaporizhzhia, the Ukrainian military claims to have [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1597262847352135681][struck Russian positions]] near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.4716287,36.2285663,11z][Polohy]], causing significant casualties
- Ukrainian forces also claim to have [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1597286676858298368][struck a railway bridge]] at [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.1144569,35.4739165,11z][Starobohdanivka]]
- The US Department of Defense is [[https://www.reuters.com/business/aerospace-defense/100-mile-strike-weapon-weighed-ukraine-arms-makers-wrestle-with-demand-sources-2022-11-28/][considering]] giving Ukraine the [[https://www.boeing.co.kr/resources/ko_KR/Seoul-International/2015/GLSDB.pdf][Ground Launched Small Diameter Bomb]] (GLSDB)
  - Combines the GBU-39 small-diameter bomb with the rocket motor from the M26 MLRS
  - 150km range, as compared to 70km with current GMLRS
  - Less capable than the 300km ATACMS, but is still a useful improvement over Ukraine's current capabilities
  - Cheap and takes advantage of weapons that the US has a significant inventory of
- New York Times [[https://www.nytimes.com/2022/11/27/world/europe/ukraine-war-bakhmut.html][article]] detailing the fighting in and around Bakhmut
  - Russia has intensified its efforts near Bakhmut
  - Russia has redeployed troops from Kherson to Bakhmut
  - Attempts to advance near Bakhmut appear to be driven more by political consideration than military necessity
- Footage of a [[https://twitter.com/Osinttechnical/status/1597079336234143745][Ukrainian command center]] in Bakhmut
  - Apparently they're sharing drone video via Google Meet
- The Russian government intends to [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1597280734460674048][issue domestic TLS certificates]] to substitute for foreign certificate authorities that have pulled out because of sanctions
- The Russian interior ministry reports a [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1597149982192463872][significant increase in gun crimes]], which is being blamed on the availability of stolen guns and ammunition from military sources
  - Apparently a common way to smuggle these weapons is with fake humanitarian charities, which bring supplies to the front and then smuggle weapons on the way back
  - Many mobilized troops are being issued weapons without their serial numbers being registered, which makes smuggling easier

** 2022-11-27 Sunday
- Near Svatove, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1596934154846842880][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.4794448,37.889303,11z][Stelmakhivka]]
- Russian sources are [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1596934158819151872][reporting additional Ukrainian offensives]] near Svatove, but there is no confirmation of this from Ukrainian sources
- Near Bakhmut/Siversk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1596934164489859072][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271337,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8603712,38.1878152,11z][Verkhnokamyanske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8075094,38.2507431,11z][Spirne]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.554042,38.012325,11z][Opytne]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6605513,38.0876815,11z][Bakhmutske]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7145913,38.1364423,11z][Yakolivka]]
- Near Donetsk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1596934170948775936][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.087187,37.5934123,11z][Pervomaiske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0095154,37.467888,11z][Krasnohorivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0572476,37.5736284,14z][Nevelske]]
- The Russians are likely [[https://twitter.com/Tatarigami_UA/status/1596941454194057217][building up for another assault]] on the [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.7544122,37.2092803,11z][Pavlivka]]/[[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.7790919,37.2438917,11z][Vuhledar]] area
- Jack Watling has a good thread on [[https://twitter.com/Jack_Watling/status/1596698941852033025][the influence of cold weather on operations]]
  - Cold weather will hamper both sides
    - Troops cannot stay outdoors for as long
    - Greater need for hot food and areas to warm up in
    - Harder to stay dry, and staying dry becomes more important
  - However, cold weather will likely hurt the Russian army more
    - Ukrainian forces appear to be more disciplined, especially at the platoon/company level
    - This discipline is key to ensuring that soldiers remain free of cold-related injuries and illnesses
    - Russian troops didn't have great small-unit leadership at the start of this war, and what leadership they did have has been depleted by the past year's fighting
  - Ukraine can inflict heavy casualties on the Russian military by skirmishing
  - Russian will be more dependent on fixed logistics nodes which can be targeted by long-range weapons (/but only if Ukraine has the range to hit those nodes --- hence the need for ATACMS/)
  - Logistics in winter will be road-bound, slowing the pace of operations on both sides
  - There will be a reduction in movement as winter sets in, but not necessarily a reduction in the intensity of fighting nor a reduction in the rate of consumption of ammunition and supplies
- This is what the [[https://www.google.com/maps/@46.6619976,32.7291459,13z][Antonovskiy Bridge]] [[https://twitter.com/WarInUkraineYet/status/1596961688473194496][looks like today]]
- There has been a [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1596819562443726848][mass outbreak of an unknown respiratory illness]], possibly COVID, at a training camp for mobilized soldiers in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@56.8320858,62.4714699,11z][Elanskii, Sverdlosk Oblast]]

** 2022-11-25 Friday
- Near Svatove, the Ukrainians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1596198280009875456][stopped attacks]] on [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.4794448,37.889303,11z][Stelmakhivka]] and near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.995738,38.098652,11z][Dibrova]] (Dibrova appears to be contested, but not yet liberated)
- Near Bakhmut, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1596198289157738496][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7329274,38.2110851,11z][Bilohorivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7145913,38.1364423,11z][Yakolivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6605513,38.0876815,11z][Bakhmutske]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.554042,38.012325,11z][Opytne]]
- Near Donetsk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1596198296422432770][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.087187,37.5934123,11z][Pervomaiske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0095154,37.467888,11z][Krasnohorivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.8534122,37.4742253,11z][Novomykhailivka]]
- Good thread on [[https://twitter.com/Tatarigami_UA/status/1596180935711465472][the role of tanks in the war]]
  - The Russian military is adapting to the new realities of the conflict in Ukraine and are using their tanks are more effectively now than they were at the start of the war
  - Russian troops have picked up on the Ukraininan tactic of using quadcopter drones to spot for and correct long-range tank fire
  - This allows tanks to serve both direct and indirect fire --- tanks can hit targets 4-6km away, even without line of sight
  - Tanks remain useful cor clearing fortified positions in urban terrain --- this was especially evident in the siege of Mariupol
  - Measures to clear and avoid anti-tank mines have improved on the Russian side
  - Artillery is generally ineffective against tanks unless it scores a direct hit
  - A tank is like a Swiss army knife on the battlefield --- may not be the perfect weapon in any given scenario, but is broadly useful in a wide range of situations
  - Not obsolete!
- US artillery [[https://www.nytimes.com/2022/11/25/us/ukraine-artillery-breakdown.html][is wearing out]] due from overuse in Ukraine
  - Ukrainian soldiers are firing thousands of rounds of artillery
  - This is wearing out the gun barrels
  - Ukrainian military is having to ship artillery pieces to Poland so they can be repaired by US technicians
  - /US artillery was never meant to operate in the way that the Ukrainians are using it/
  - /In the US military doctrine, tube artillery is meant to be supplemented by air power --- this is modeled off Israeli tactics during the 1973 Arab-Israeli War/
  - /As a result, US artillery emphasizes mobility and maneuver over durability --- parts are built with titanium rather than steel/
  - /However, Ukraine doesn't have the same air power capacity that the US or Western European countries do, which means that Ukrainians are much more reliant on artillery/
- A German-delivered [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1596148685372624897][MARS II MLRS]] in Ukraine
  - /Tracked vehicles are proving their utility in Ukrainian mud/
- Norway has [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1596145510687346688][announced more military aid]] for Ukraine
  - Most notable is the spare parts for the M109 self-propelled howitzers they sent earlier
- A [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1596089912322932743][possible bombing]] at the Russian civil administration building in Mariupol
- (Follow-up from 2022-11-23) Vladimir Putin has [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1596213028923768832][ordered the creation]] of a unified military mobilization database, presumably to streamline future mobilization efforts
  - Database will unify data from tax services and the health ministry, as well as pre-existing military databases
  - Database will track who has had prior military experience
- Russian troops [[https://twitter.com/wartranslated/status/1596115247898787840][review]] the canned food they are sent
- A group of people identified as Ukrainian saboteurs and killed by the FSB [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1596066963608178688][were reportedly a group of video game enthusiasts engaged in a live-action role play]]
- A Russian pro-military channel [[https://twitter.com/wartranslated/status/1596175436811472897][defends]] the mobilized troops from Serpukhov
  - Castigates critics for writing from the warmth and safety of their homes as they blame people stuck in harsh conditions for fleeing
  - Asks where was the artillery and heavy weapons support for this hapless unit
  - Says that mobilized soldiers don't owe civilian critics anything

  - There are indications of a troop build-up in southern Donetsk, indicating a possible attack in the coming days
- [[https://www.google.com/maps/@46.649626,32.5727624,11z][Kherson City]] [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1595849202533384195][was shelled by Russia]], resulting in civilian casualties
- Russian troops say that experience in Syria [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1595732208010072064][did not provide adequate training or preparation for Ukraine]]
- [[https://twitter.com/SamBendett/status/1595788630206849024][Good thread]] on the Russian war effort by the director of a Russian non-governmental organization providing support to troops
  - Difference in the usage of small drones in Ukraine highlights the lack of multi-domain coordination and integration in the Russian military
  - American "gadgets" (i.e. precision munitions) are effective --- Russia had underestimated the battlefield utility of precision munitions prior to the war
  - Russian forces are made acutely aware of their deficiencies w.r.t. information processing --- takes a long time for battlefield reports to get turned into artillery/air strikes
  - Argues that many more people need to be mobilized in order to storm Ukrainian defenses in Donetsk
- The fact that Russia is having to use physical attacks to hit Ukrainian electrical infrastructure is a sign that Ukraine's electricity grid is [[https://mas.to/@dmitri/109400403574511659][hardened against cyber-attack]] in a way that it wasn't in 2014
- According to The Guardian, [[https://www.theguardian.com/world/2022/nov/24/iranian-military-advisers-killed-aiding-moscow-in-crimea-kyiv][Iranian military advisers were assassinated in Crimea]]
- 27 hours after being disrupted by a Russian attack, [[https://twitter.com/ukraine_map/status/1595773680604299266][water has been restored]] in Kyiv
- [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1595702653706973184][The value of pro-war memorabilia is falling]] in Russia, with items having to be discounted or withdrawn from sale entirely
  - The decline in value of items with pro-war logos reportedly accelerated after the Russian retreat from Kherson
- Ukraine has [[https://twitter.com/wartranslated/status/1595696830595362818][disconnected its nuclear power plants from the electricity grid]], because the sudden load fluctuations caused by Russian strikes were causing undue stress on the reactors
- The mobilized troops from Serpukhov (see 2022-11-23) [[https://twitter.com/wartranslated/status/1595721613604962307][are receiving little sympathy]]

** 2022-11-23 Wednesday
- Near Siversk, Russian forces [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1595484084129910784][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271337,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8075094,38.2507431,11z][Spirne]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7634233,38.2371188,11z][Berestove]]

  - Russians also attacked [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.3921847,37.9034419,12z][Pivnichne]]
  - /Pivnichne is near Shumy, which has shown up in the fighting before, although not recently/
- Near Donetsk, Russia [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1595484097736065036][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.2489705,37.7731833,11z][Novobakhmutivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.087187,37.5934123,11z][Pervomaiske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0572476,37.5736284,14z][Nevelske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0095154,37.467888,11z][Krasnohorivka]]
  - Reports of Russian progress in Marinka, although it doesn't seem like they have full control over the town yet
- Reports of [[https://twitter.com/TCG_CrisisRisks/status/1595297060634259458][increased Russian shelling]] in the [[https://www.google.com/maps/@50.9006602,34.7791948,11z][Sumy]] area
  - /Not sure what's going on here/
  - /Sumy has been quiet since the Russians retreated in March/
- A Russian rocket reportedly [[https://twitter.com/Osinttechnical/status/1595297412058423298][hit a maternity ward]] in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9435282,35.4251762,11z][Vilnyansk]], Zaporizhzhia Oblast
- The EU has designated Russia [[https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/european-lawmakers-declare-russia-state-sponsor-terrorism-2022-11-23/][as a state sponsor of terrorism]]
- [[https://twitter.com/WarInUkraineYet/status/1595394709324984320][More power outages]] in Kyiv as Russian missiles continue to strike Ukrainian electricity and heating infrastructure
  - /I don't understand the logic behind these Russian attacks/
  - /The evidence from World War 2 shows that random strikes on civilian infrastructure do little to demoralize the enemy, and will probably have the opposite effect, hardening resistance/
  - /At least in World War 2, some of these attacks could be justified because they were seen as hurting the enemy's production capacity, but this isn't even having that effect because Ukraine is getting its weapons from outside the country/
- Apparently Russian attacks on power infrastructure in Ukraine has led to [[https://twitter.com/WarInUkraineYet/status/1595400336952393728][power outages in Moldova]]
- According to an independent Russian news outlet, there are plans for a [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1595377037451083776][second wave of mobilization]] over the winter
  - No plans for a general mobilization, because Russian authorities have recognized that the military does not have the logistical capacity to equip that many new recruits
  - Russia is also reportedly reorganizing its mobilization database, and is in the process of improving its links to other government databases in order to more effectively track people eligible for mobilization
- According to an independent Russian news source, mobilized Russian soldiers near Svatove are being [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1595396554155823112][denied medical care]] unless they agree to return to the front
- Mobilized Russian troops seen fighting [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1595213326249861121][with World War 2 era helmets]]
- A [[https://twitter.com/wartranslated/status/1595515700810027008][long video]] filmed by mobilized troops from [[https://www.google.com/maps/@54.9225137,37.3944399,11z][Serpukhov]]
  - Complain about poor leadership and equipment
  - Repeatedly complain about officers running away under fire
  - The equipment that they do receive is substandard, such as body armor that's only meant to protect against airsoft pellets, and helmets that can be cracked open with a knife
- Yet [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1595562318141743105][another account]] describing the experience of mobilized troops, this time by troops from [[https://www.google.com/maps/@52.9743919,36.0076967,11z][Oryol]]
  - Similar complaints re: lack of weapons and training
    - No anti-tank weapons
    - Troops had few weapons --- one recruit didn't even know how to change the magazine on his rifle
  - Troops retreated to Svatove, where they were taken into custody by military police
  - A general said that they had to go back to the front, otherwise they would be referred for judicial proceedings
  - Were forced to stay in a forest without food for five days
  - Then were transported to Zaitseve, where they were held in a basement and fed only one meal per day
- Kamil Galeev has a [[https://twitter.com/kamilkazani/status/1595456040677556226][Twitter thread]] with more details about how Ramzan Kadyrov rules Chechnya as an autonomous province with the blessing of Putin
  - Chechnya is best viewed as a monarchy
  - More functional and less corrupt, in many ways, than the rest of Russia, especially the other North Caucasus provinces, such as Dagestan
  - Saying that Chechnya is a "tribal" society is just Orientalism --- Chechen tribes are akin to modern Scottish clans --- useful as symbols and reminders of heritage, but don't play a part in the political process
  - Kadyrov values personal loyalty over family ties --- has elevated deputies who have killed for him with their own hands over family members
- Biden administration officials are concerned that Russia [[https://www.politico.com/news/2022/11/23/russia-chemical-weapons-ukraine-00070743][may use chemical weapons]] in Ukraine
  - /This is disturbingly plausible/
  - /The area around Bakhmut has been stalemated for more than six months/
  - /In World War 1, both German and Entente armies used gas weapons to try to break the stalemate/
