- Iran's provision of UAVs to Russia may be [[https://twitter.com/HoansSolo/status/1594247650777657345][part of a bid]] to secure advanced fighter aircraft for itself
- The Wall Street Journal has a [[https://www.wsj.com/articles/ukraines-kherson-win-shifts-dynamics-across-whole-front-with-russia-11668914888][good analysis]] of the impact and future implications of Ukraine's victory at Kherson city
  - Unlike the withdrawal from Kharkiv, the Russian withdrawal from Kherson was orderly --- Russia was able to salvage a great deal of equipment, and was able to destroy whatever equipment it couldn't withdraw
  - Ukrainian forces continue to maintain the initiative
  - The recapture of Kherson city enables Ukrainian forces to target Russian supply lines into the remainder of Kherson oblast with long-range weapons, such as HIMARS
  - US officials say it's clear that Ukrainian forces have a greater will to fight than Russian forces
  - The US has indicated that it does not consider Crimea to be Russian territory --- US will not object to Ukrainian strikes on Crimea
- Ukrainian mud [[https://twitter.com/Osinttechnical/status/1594456414583398402][is nuts]]

** 2022-11-19 Saturday
- Near Siversk, Russia [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1594035688185499648][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271337,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8603712,38.1878152,11z][Verkhnokamyanske]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8075094,38.2507431,11z][Spirne]]
- Near Bakhmut, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1594035756925743106][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.5279761,37.9495319,11z][Klishchiivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4682884,37.9557667,11z][Kurdyumivka]]
- Near Donetsk, the Russans [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1594035772901888000][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0970994,37.6616264,11z][Vodyane]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.087187,37.5934123,11z][Pervomaiske]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.8534122,37.4742253,11z][Novomykhailivka]]
- It appears that the Ukrainians have [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1594035776635162625][retreated]] from [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.7544122,37.2092803,11z][Pavlivka]]
- According to US officials, Iran and Russia have [[https://www.washingtonpost.com/national-security/2022/11/19/russia-iran-drones-secret-deal/][struck a deal]] to produce Iranian UAVs inside Russia
  - Will help address Russia's shortage of precision-guided munitions
  - Iran believes that it can avert sanctions if the munitions are built in Russia, and Iran merely provides the designs/intellectual property
- [[https://www.nytimes.com/2022/11/18/us/politics/ukraine-russia-missiles.html][Another story]] on Russian usage of precision-guided munitions
  - Russia has increased its imports of precision-guided munitions from Iran and North Korea
  - Evidence that Russia had stockpiled microelectronic components from before the war
  - Smuggling --- obtaining dual use electronic components through front companies
  - Using weapons outside their intended design parameters
    - Anti-ship missiles used for ground attack
    - Anti-aircraft missiles used as indiscriminate bombardment weapons
  - Using weapons from reserve stockpiles that had been held back in anticipation of a larger conflict with NATO --- /now that the Ukraine War has "settled down", somewhat, and the chances of it turning into a wider conflict appear less likely, the Russian military leadership may feel more comfortable allocating "emergency reserve" weapons to the war in Ukraine/
- Michael Kofman has [[https://twitter.com/KofmanMichael/status/1593979976793088001][more thoughts]] on the effects of sanctions on the Russian military industry
  - Sanctions will have effects, but they'll have effects through second and third order mechanisms
  - For example: Western sanctions mean no more machine tools going into Russia
  - But the effect of that sanction will only be felt when existing Russian machine tools wear out and break down
- [[https://www.spiegel.de/politik/deutschland/ukraine-panzerhaubitzen-2000-wegen-ersatzteilmangels-ausser-gefecht-a-a9056b03-3c01-40cb-b495-611817741b21][According to Der Spiegel]] (use Google Translate), procurement issues with spare parts for the PzH 2000 have affected their availability for Ukraine
  - /Once again, the US DoD's procurement system is the worst... except for all our allies'/

** 2022-11-16 Wednesday
- Near Siversk, Russia [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1592965534639099904][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7329274,38.2110851,11z][Bilohorivka]]
- [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1592965541186400256][No attacks]] near Bakhmut
- Donetsk
  - Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1592965548555792384][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.1451452,37.727358,11z][Avdiivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.2481406,37.6891264,11z][Novokalynove]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0970994,37.6616264,11z][Vodyane]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.087187,37.5934123,11z][Pervomaiske]]
  - It seems like the Russians have [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1592965548555792384][given up on]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.7544122,37.2092803,11z][Pavlivka]]
- Apparently the offensive on Pavlivka was conducted with [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1592965552322260992][without any preparatory diversionary attacks]], allowing Ukrainian defenders to concentrate their fires
- The missile that landed in Poland was apparently a [[https://twitter.com/seungminkim/status/1592745092112347136][Ukrainian interceptor that malfunctioned]]
  - [[https://twitter.com/UAWeapons/status/1592629251161075712][Investigation]] by Ukraine Weapons Tracker that identified the missile
- [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1592988548499578880][Explosions]] heard in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@45.7095902,34.3846662,11z][Dzhankoi, Crimea]]
- The performance of NASAMs is [[https://twitter.com/jseldin/status/1592939683407073280][impressive]], according to the US Defense Department
- [[https://kyivindependent.com/national/michael-kofman-after-kherson-gains-for-ukraine-will-come-at-slower-pace][Analysis]] by Michael Kofman on the war thus far
  - Ukraine will difficulty taking more terrain in Kherson Oblast this winter because of weather constraints and more entrenched Russian defenses
  - Potential for more Ukrainian gains in Luhansk, contingent on how well Russian infrastructure can supply troops in the field over there
  - The more Ukraine gains, the harder it will be for them to make more gains because Russian forces will have less and less area to defend
  - The Ukrainian approach to taking Kherson favored preserving Ukrainian troops and the city --- Russian forces were allowed to leave without a pitched battle
  - Russia handled the retreat from Kherson better than it handled the retreat from Kharkiv, both in terms of organization and PR
- According to Russian human rights activists, Wagner has [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1592981715458600961][executed at least 40 of its own soldiers]] in Ukraine
  - Wagner has recruited 35,000 - 40,000 prisoners
  - Reports of Wagner conscripting people from prison --- this contradicts Prigozhin's own claims that he wanted volunteers
  - Prisoners are reportedly being beaten and tortured into signing contracts
  - Any official inquiries into Wagner's recruitment are met with a response that indicates that details are state secrets

** 2022-11-15 Tuesday
- Near Svatove, the Ukrainians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1592592372738985985][repulsed an attack]] on [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.5222553,37.9480571,13z][Novoselivske]]
- Near Bakhmut, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1592592386143956992][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7329274,38.2110851,11z][Bilohorivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6605513,38.0876815,11z][Bakhmutske]]
  - /I still don't understand the purpose of the near constant attacks on Bakhmut/

- The US announced another [[https://twitter.com/ukraine_map/status/1590829680927686656][$400 million aid package for Ukraine]]
  - More precision-guided artillery ammunition
  - More HIMARS ammunition
  - More Humvees
  - 4 Avenger air-defense systems --- the Avenger uses Stinger missiles, but carries more of them and is on the back of a Humvee
    - /This will be especially useful against slower and lower flying targets like loitering munitions/
  - Hawk air defense systems
    - /Interesting because the US phased out Hawk in 1994/
    - /Launchers are probably coming from Spain, which still uses the system, with missiles being supplied by the US/

** 2022-11-11 Friday
- Good [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1591192952923369472][analysis thread]] on the liberation of Kherson
  - The goal for Ukraine is to liberate territory, not kill Russians
  - If this means allowing Russian forces to retreat, that's fine, if it saves Ukrainian lives
  - That said, Ukraine did not just let Russians leave --- the retreat was the result of months of Ukrainian bombardment and slow grinding offensives
  - Just like the liberation of Kharkiv Oblast, the offensive in Kherson demonstrates the of Ukraine to liberate territory, and helps solidify Western support
- Near Svatove, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1591143877234561024][attempted to counterattack]] at [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.5222553,37.9480571,13z][Novoselivske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.4426256,37.8983083,12z][Miasozharivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.2200192,37.9465744,11z][Makiivka]]
- Near Bakhmut, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1591143886390718464][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271478,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.746171,38.1475132,11z][Vesele]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6969475,38.0538431,11z][Soledar]]
- In Donetsk Oblast, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1591143891868475392][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.087187,37.5934123,11z][Pervomaiske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0572476,37.5736284,14z][Nevelske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.7544122,37.2092803,11z][Pavlivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0095154,37.467888,11z][Krasnohorivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0959777,37.719841,11z][Opytne]]

** 2022-11-05 Saturday
- The Ukrainian offensive near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.4093066,38.1445444,11z][Svatove]] [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1588972332076257280][appears to have stalled]]
- Near Siversk the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1588972338158395392][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271478,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8075094,38.2507431,11z][Spirne]]
- Near Bakhmut, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1588972348211810304][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6605655,38.0876815,11z][Bakhmutske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.5540349,38.012325,11z][Opytne]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.5029324,38.0153435,11z][Odradivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.451971,37.9454831,11z][Ozarianivka]]
- The Russians are continuing to [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1588972356936290305][press their attack]] near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.7544122,37.2092803,11z][Pavlivka]]
- Still no news out of Kherson, just [[https://twitter.com/COUPSURE/status/1588924419002740736][rumors and inferences from satellite imagery]]
  - Russians are building fortifications on the left side of the Dnipro river
  - Pre-fabricated bunkers are exclusively behind the city of Kherson, indicating a set pre-built defensive fortifications that the Russians would retreat to
- Apparently [[https://twitter.com/Tatarigami_UA/status/1588927961138597889][additional troops have arrived]] in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@53.1271998,25.9668923,8z][Baranovichi, Belarus]]
  - /Seems like this is that joint Russian-Belarussian training program/
- Soldiers from Russia's Rostov Oblast [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1588672503832268800][posted a video]] claiming poor supplies and leadership, this video was taken down and the journalist who publicized it was prosecuted
  - /One thing I don't understand is the lack of mutinies among Russian soldiers, if conditions are this poor/
  - /We are hearing about soldiers refusing to fight, but it doesn't seem to be occurring on a large enough scale to be hurting the Russian military's ability to conduct combat operations/
  - /On the other hand, given the over incompetence and uselessness of the Russian military in this war, how would we even know? Especially if the threat of mutiny causes Russian officers to not undertake attacks that they might have taken --- it's difficult to prove a counterfactual/

** 2022-11-03 Thursday
- Near Kreminna and Siversk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1588249278199189505][launched attacks]] on [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.2199911,37.9465744,11z][Makiivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1669387,37.9575929,11z][Nevske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271478,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8603712,38.1878152,11z][Verkhnokamyanka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8075094,38.2507431,11z][Spirne]]
  - Shelling was also reported in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.2061799,38.0825557,11z][Ploshchanka]]
  - /It looks like the Russians have shifted focus away from Bakhmut, to around Kreminna in the north and Pavlivka in the south/
- Near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6040205,37.9752039,11z][Bakhmut]], Russian attacks were once again [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1588249283702112256][very sporadic]]
- In South Donetsk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1588249289905811457][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.7544122,37.2092803,11z][Pavlivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.7808401,37.0617733,11z][Prechystivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0970994,37.6616264,11z][Vodyane]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.8534122,37.4742253,11z][Novomykhailivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0871584,37.5934123,11z][Pervomaiske]]
- Russia appears to be doing [[https://twitter.com/KofmanMichael/status/1588160963572035584][whatever it can to hold the Svatove-Kreminna line]], including [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1587882645874155521][sending in conscripts with little to no training, equipment or leadership]]
- Reuters [[https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/heavily-criticised-russian-commander-takes-three-week-holiday-agency-says-2022-11-03/][confirms]] the dismissal of General Lapin, citing Russian sources that claim that the general is on a "three week holiday"
- /The news out of Kherson is very conflicted/
  - /On the one hand, we have Russian forces bringing in [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1587426043484323847][pre-fabricated fortifications]], and digging secondary and tertiary defensive trenches/
  - /On the other hand, we have what appears to be the Russian occupation authorities [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1588107211837956096][departing the main civil administration building]], and Russian Telegram channels claiming [[https://twitter.com/wartranslated/status/1588203897629319169][troops are being evacuated]]/
- [[https://www.ft.com/content/14ea4d75-b273-4a89-8a3f-c7708881673b][Reporting]] on the state of Ukraine's civilian and military infrastructure going into the winter
  - Russian loitering munition strikes have had an effect
  - Ukraine has told some refugees not to return during the winter, in order to reduce demand for electricity
  - However, the Ukrainian military appears to have ample supplies of fuel and cold-weather gear

** 2022-11-02 Wednesday
- Near Svatove and Kreminna, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1587867852316594176][launched counterattacks]] near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.2199911,37.9465744,11z][Makiivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1669387,37.9575929,11z][Nevske]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271478,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]]
- [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1587867857462910976][Very little to report]] near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6040205,37.9752039,11z][Bakhmut]]
  - It appears that Russia has reallocated forces towards Pavlivka
- In South Donetsk, the Ukrainians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1587867868967976960][repelled attacks]] on [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0871584,37.5934123,11z][Pervomaiske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.8534122,37.4742253,11z][Novomykhailivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.7544122,37.2092803,11z][Pavlivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.7808401,37.0617733,11z][Prechystivka]]
- In Russia, mobilized troops reportedly [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1587793590406848512][protested a lack of pay]], and had to be dispersed by Rosgvardia

** 2022-11-01 Tuesday
- Not much to report from Svatove/Kreminna, as the Ukrainians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1587502951656030210][launched attacks]] towards [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.0974123,38.1786402,11z][Zhytlivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.6420886,37.8921433,11z][Kyslivka]], but the Ukrainians don't appear to have captured too much additional territory
- Near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.7544122,37.2092803,11z][Pavlivka]], the Russians are [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1587502962276016128][pushing hard]] and have reportedly made progress towards capturing the highway through [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.7808401,37.0617733,11z][Prechystivka]]
- Russia's [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1587461115256135682][fall draft has begun]], and the MoD has stated that these conscripts will not be sent to Ukraine
- Russian forces are [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1587426043484323847][moving pre-fabricated concrete pillboxes]] into Kherson
- Belarus continues to [[https://twitter.com/NOELreports/status/1587428073129082881][send tanks and other military equipment]] to Russia

** 2022-10-31 Monday
- [[https://wiki.quanticle.net/Main/SouthwardsAndEastwardPressureOnRussianForces][War on the Rocks podcast]]
- Russia and Belarus [[https://twitter.com/nexta_tv/status/1587227977468858370][sign an agreement]] to create joint training centers for conscripted Russian troops
  - /This makes sense for Russia, because many of the Russian forces that would have been dedicated to training new conscripts have themselves been deployed to Ukraine/
- Near Kharkiv, Russia [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1587161842983526400][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@50.2233243,36.5783157,11z][Zelene]]
- On the Svatove-Kreminna front, [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1587161848478158849][shelling was reported]] near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.2061799,38.0825557,11z][Ploshchanka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1314083,38.1373012,11z][Chervonopopivka]], indicating a Ukrainian presence in that area
- The Ukrainians also [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1587161853905469441][fought off a Russian counterattack]] near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.5222553,37.9480571,13z][Novoselivske]], indicating that they have positions close by
- Near Siversk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1587161853905469441][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271478,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7720518,38.3182918,11z][Mykolaivka]]
  - /The report of fighting in Mykolaivka is very surprising, because the last time there was any fighting reported there was in June/
  - /I thought that the Russians had captured it as part of their initial push out of Severodonentsk and Lysychansk/
- Near Bakhmut, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1587161864294879233][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6605655,38.0876815,11z][Bakhmutske]]
- Near Donetsk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1587161870691090433][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.1451452,37.727358,11z][Avdiivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0623636,37.7116655,11z][Vesele]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0970994,37.6616264,11z][Vodyane]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.2489705,37.7731833,11z][Novobakhmutivka]]
  - /Novobakhmutivka is a new town to show up on the list of attacked towns, but it's near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.2845451,37.7678517,11z][Oleksandropil]], which was a site of heavy fighting in August/
- Near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.7544122,37.2092803,11z][Pavlivka]], the large scale Russian attack [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1587161876085051394][is ongoing]], but it doesn't seem like the Russians have been very successful at capturing any settlements
  - Russian channels are reporting that the Ukrainians have brought reinforcements to the area

** 2022-10-30 Sunday
- Ukrainian forces [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1586792370913288203][appear to have advanced]] to the outskirts of [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1314083,38.1373012,11z][Chervonopopivka]], near Kremmina
- Near Bakhmut, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1586792383823347712][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7145913,38.1364423,11z][Yakolivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6605655,38.0876815,11z][Bakhmutske]]
  - /Reportedly, the Ukrainians have made some incremental advances here, reversing some recent Russian incremental gains/
  - /Overall, though, this fight looks like a stalemate to me, with neither side having the strength to force a breakthrough or conduct a large counterattack/
- Near Donetsk
  - It appears that the Russians have [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1586792391117258753][made some marginal progress]] near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0970994,37.6616264,11z][Vodyane]]
  - Russia also [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1586792391117258753][launched the usual round of attacks]] against [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.1729265,37.7814818,11z][Kamyanka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.1451452,37.727358,11z][Avdiivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0871584,37.5934123,11z][Pervomaiske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0095154,37.467888,11z][Krasnohorivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.8534122,37.4742253,11z][Novomykhailivka]]
- Heavy fighting is also ongoing near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.7790919,37.2438917,11z][Vuhledar]], with the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1586792396645351424][launching a large attack]] on [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.7544122,37.2092803,11z][Pavlivka]]
  - /This area of the front had been quiet for almost a full month, and now the Russians have launched two attacks here in as many days/
  - /Could this be the result of new conscript units arriving?/
- Still no word out of Kherson, but it seems like Russia is continuing to [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1586792401930264578][entrench and reinforce]]
- Italy and France will [[https://twitter.com/ukraine_map/status/1586716393877438464][supply Ukraine]] with SAMP-T air defense systems
- Mobilized Russian conscripts [[https://twitter.com/wartranslated/status/1586858112975241217][review their weapons]]
  - /I'm no expert on guns, but I'm pretty sure that recoil springs aren't supposed to be rusty/

** 2022-10-29 Saturday
- [[https://www.google.com/maps/@46.6844949,32.4965447,12z][Chornobaivka airfield]], northwest of Kherson, has [[https://twitter.com/TCG_CrisisRisks/status/1586207092842516480][reportedly been abandoned by Russian forces]]
- [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1586394389026377730][Not much news]] out of the Kreminna/Svatove region
- [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1586394395611234304][Not much to report]] from Bakhmut
- Near Donetsk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1586394401210740737][launched attacks]] on [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0970994,37.6616264,11z][Vodyane]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0575356,37.5777002,15z][Nevelske]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.1729265,37.7814818,11z][Kamyanka]]
- [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1586394408764997634][Heavy fighting]] reported near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.7790919,37.2438917,11z][Vuhledar]]
  - /This is the first fighting reported in that area in almost a month/
- [[https://twitter.com/COUPSURE/status/1586354604815446018][Footage]] of the unmanned surface vehicle attack against the Black Sea fleet in Sevastopol
  - The USV attack reportedly [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1586310179112759296][resulted in minor damage]] to the minesweeper /Ivan Golubets/
- As a result of the attack, Russia has [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1586374626493751297][ended its participation]] in the agreement that allowed the continued export of Ukrainian grain
- According to RIA Novosti, the head of the central military district, Col. Gen. Alexander Lapin has been [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1586350383370117120][relieved of command]]
  - According to Russian Telegram channels, the relief was reportedly due to the poor employment of conscript units
  - Reports were that conscripts were getting sent into combat without adequate training or equipment
  - Lapin had recently come under heavy criticism from both Evgeny Prigozhin and Ramzan Kadyrov
  - Lapin's removal means that all five of the commanders who initially led the invasion [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1586362892969967618][have been relieved]]
  - Lapin's [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1586375621646614529][replacement]] is Col. Gen. Sergei Kuzovlev
  - Lapin reportedly [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1586488705745047552][threatened to shoot]] a lieutenant who withdrew his platoon without authorization

** 2022-10-28 Friday
- Russia has reportedly [[https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/russia-hits-ukraine-homes-evacuates-kherson-warns-escalation-2022-10-24/][completed its mobilization]]
- According to Serhey Haidai, the Ukrainian governor of Luhansk Oblast, Ukrainian forces have [[https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/ukrainian-forces-largely-control-key-road-east-says-kyiv-2022-10-28/][captured the P66 highway]] connecting [[https://goo.gl/maps/SXSJYZ6ZCKufv6gP9][Kreminna]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.4093066,38.1445444,11z][Svatove]]
- Russia warns that it may [[https://www.reuters.com/world/russia-says-wests-commercial-satellites-could-be-targets-2022-10-27/][attack commercial satellites]] if they're involved in the Ukraine War
- Near Svatove, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1586048226616283136][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.4246428,37.9013316,12z][Andriivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271337,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]]
  - Ukrainian forces [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1586048226616283136][may have entered]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.5397758,37.8912212,12z][Berestove]], but that is still unconfirmed
- Near Kreminna, [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1586048232828055553][Russian sources indicated fighting]] in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1224694,38.171178,12z][Pishchane]], indicating a possible Ukrainian advance in the area
  - /Note that this is still an unconfirmed rumor/
- Near Bakhmut, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1586048246786318340][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6605513,38.0876815,11z][Bakhmutske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6969192,38.0538431,11z][Soledar]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4750907,37.9636501,13z][Zelenopillya]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7145771,38.1364423,11z][Yakolivka]]
  - /Zelenopillya appears to be a new town under attack, but it's right next to [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4682884,37.9557667,11z][Kurdyumivka]], so it's not surprising that the Russians are attacking there as well/
- Near Donetsk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1586048253623238658][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0871584,37.5934123,11z][Pervomaiske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.2489705,37.7731833,11z][Novobakhmutivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0575356,37.5777002,15z][Nevelske]]
- Farther west, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1586048258568507392][launched an attack]] on [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.8205,36.8549072,12z][Vremivka]], attacking in an area of the front which had been fairly calm over the past few weeks
- [[https://twitter.com/NOELreports/status/1585293554225586177][Visual confirmation]] of the liberation of [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1669387,37.9575929,11z][Nevske]], which had been reported liberated on 2022-10-24
- Today marks the [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1585731413340434432][1-year anniversary]] of the beginning of the build-up for the war

** 2022-10-27 Thursday
- Near Bakhmut, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1585696314179846166][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271337,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.5556744,38.0241382,13z][Ivanhrad]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6969192,38.0538431,11z][Soledar]]
- Near Donetsk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1585696329426141228][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0095154,37.467888,11z][Krasnohorivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]]
- Wagner is [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1585604494972186624][recruiting operators]] for a variety of high-end weapons systems including Pantsir air defense systems, helicopters and Su-25 ground attack jets
  - Wagner is increasing building itself up as a force that can operate totally independently of the Russian military
  - /Is this a deliberate strategy on the part of Putin to build up Wagner as a praetorian guard to defend him from a potential rebellion or palace coup from the military?/
- The fuel depot in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0624422,38.4180699,11z][Shakhtarsk, Donetsk]] was actually a [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1585440104285356033][train carrying fuel]]
- [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1585543112641896448][Video]] of the destruction in Marinka
- [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1585516240080195585][Low flying Ukrainian Su-25s]]
- The photos that Russia is using in its propaganda alleging that Ukraine is preparing a dirty bomb are [[https://twitter.com/govSlovenia/status/1584936237806206976][actually from Slovenia]]
- The head of Wagner, Dmitry Prigozhin, has reportedly [[https://www.washingtonpost.com/national-security/2022/10/25/putin-insider-prigozhin-blasts-russian-generals-ukraine/][told Putin personally]] that his generals are doing a poor job

** 2022-10-26 Wednesday
- On October 24, the governor of Belgorod Oblast announced that [[https://twitter.com/DefenceHQ/status/1585134337883869184][an explosive device had damaged the primary rail link between Russia and southern Belarus]]; an anti-war group called Stop The Wagons too responsibility for the attack
- Australia [[https://www.abc.net.au/news/2022-10-26/australia-will-send-troops-to-train-ukraine-forces-uk-russia-war/101581492][commits more armored vehicles and trainers]] to support Ukraine
- A fuel depot in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0624422,38.4180699,11z][Shakhtarsk, Donetsk]] has [[https://twitter.com/bayraktar_1love/status/1585342497613832193][caught fire]], presumably because of a Ukrainian attack
- Near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@50.1903834,36.6600833,11z][Ternova]], the Ukrainians reportedly [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1585324083797192704][repelled a major Russian attack]], resulting in significant armored vehicle losses
- Near Bakhmut, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1585324090692288512][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.5556744,38.0241382,13z][Ivanhrad]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6605513,38.0876815,11z][Bakhmutske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6969192,38.0538431,11z][Soledar]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4682884,37.9557667,11z][Kurdyumivka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.501002,37.9621283,14z][Andriivka]]
- Near Donetsk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1585324096703057921][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.8534122,37.4742253,11z][Novomykhailivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0575356,37.5777002,15z][Nevelske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.1729265,37.7814818,11z][Kamyanka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0095154,37.467888,11z][Krasnohorivka]]
- According to the Ukrainian general staff, [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1585324100008153089][the Kherson offensive has slowed due to bad weather]]
- Local Russian authorities are mobilizing troops [[https://twitter.com/wartranslated/status/1585350676695031808][without sending them official summons]]
  - /The person being mobilized is a teacher; which I thought was an exempt profession/
- Moscow police are reportedly [[https://twitter.com/Biz_Ukraine_Mag/status/1580866627175821312][stopping military aged males on the street and handing out mobilization notices]]
- Reuters has a good [[https://www.reuters.com/investigates/special-report/ukraine-crisis-russia-base][investigative report]] based on captured papers from the abandoned Russian headquarters in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.4591651,36.8350225,11z][Balakliya]]
  - In the weeks prior to the Russian retreat Russian units were struggling with electronic warfare and surveillance
    - Not enough drones or trained operators
    - Frequent breakdowns of jamming equipment
  - A Russian officer describes the demoralizing effect of Ukrainian artillery --- says that being in Balakliya is like "playing Russian roulette"
  - Documents describe that a Russian colonel referred to only by his callsign, Granit, was responsible for torturing local civilians
  - The commander responsible for the Balakliya area was reportedly Colonel Ivan Popov, of the 11th Army Corp, a unit attached to Russia's Baltic Fleet
  - Personnel records also show that conscripts from the Luhansk People's Republic were also present in Balakliya
    - Were responsible for local policing and garrison duties
    - Poorly manned and equipped
      - Some servicemen were in their 60s
      - One conscript required medical attention because his Mosin-Nagant rifle exploded in his hands
  - Documents also show the pay rates for Russian troops
    - A Russian sergeant serving in Balakliya was paid approximately $3200 per month, including combat bonuses
    - LPR troops were paid significantly less; a sergeant in the LPR militia was paid only $1400 a month
  - Many of the separatist troops were reported to have criminal records
  - As the Ukrainian counteroffensive in the area gathered momentum, Russia's problems with communication and discipline only worsened
  - Many senior Russian officers would give orders, only for the orders to either get lost or be disobeyed by units in the field
  - Logistics problems were also reported, with many units reporting that they were short of ammunition

** 2022-10-25 Tuesday
- Near Bakhmut, Russia [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1584946554439225345][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9271337,38.2397347,11z][Bilohorivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8603712,38.1878152,11z][Verkhnokamyanske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8075094,38.2507431,11z][Spirne]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6969192,38.0538431,11z][Soledar]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.5556744,38.0241382,13z][Ivanhrad]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.5279761,37.9495319,11z][Klishchiivka]]
- Near Donetsk, Russia [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1584946554439225345][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0575356,37.5777002,15z][Nevelske]]
- Russia is reportedly [[https://foreignpolicy.com/2022/10/25/afghanistan-russia-ukraine-military-recruitment-putin-taliban/][recruiting]] US-trained Afghan special forces soldiers to fight in Ukraine
  - Ex-Afghan National Army special forces
  - Well-regarded by the US --- were some of the few ANA units that put up meaningful resistance when the Taliban took over
  - Could not make it out of the country when the US backed Afghan government fell and US forces retreated
  - Being recruited by the Wagner group
  - Many of these ex-soldiers are refugees in Pakistan or Turkey
- [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1584988667961315328][More videos]] of mobilized Russian soliders being deployed with inadequate equipment
  - Soldiers complain about having to buy their own uniforms
  - Inadequate food and water
  - No tents
  - Lack of logistics, lack of orders
  - /This isn't all that surprising to me/
    - /Russian logistics was struggling even at the beginning of the war/
    - /Now Putin has added tens of thousands of front-line troops without increasing his army's logistical capacity/
    - /I don't understand why the Russians aren't using mobilized conscripts to drive trucks and man warehouses/
    - /Maybe the trucks and warehouses are already fully manned, and there just isn't enough organizational capacity to create more?/
    - /Maybe not enough time for training?/
- The House Progressive Caucus [[https://www.reuters.com/world/us-congress-progressives-withdraw-letter-urging-negotiations-end-ukraine-war-2022-10-25/][withdraws its letter]] after facing blowback

  - Russia [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1584611347492667392][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8075094,38.2507431,11z][Spirne]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6969192,38.0538431,11z][Soledar]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6605513,38.0876815,11z][Bakhmutske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.501002,37.9621283,14z][Andriivka]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.5279761,37.9495319,11z][Klishchiivka]]
  - /If the Russians have been pushed back, how are they still able to attack Klishchiivka?/
- Near Donetsk, the Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1584611356317143041][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.1451452,37.727358,11z][Avdiivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0871584,37.5934123,11z][Pervomaiske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.057244,37.5736284,14z][Nevelske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.8534122,37.4742253,11z][Novomykhailivka]]
- [[https://twitter.com/jabuttee/status/1584465057689505792][Video]] of a GMLRS projectile (fired from a HIMARS or similar) impacting a Russian position in the Kherson region
- US considers [[https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/exclusive-us-considers-hawk-air-defense-equipment-ukraine-say-us-officials-2022-10-25/][sending older Hawk air defense systems]] to Ukraine
  - The Hawk is the predecessor to Patriot
  - Vietnam-era ground based air defense
  - The reason we hadn't sent them to Ukraine before is because the launchers have been in storage for a long time and are thought to require significant refurbishment
- Members of the House Progressive Caucus, including Ilhan Omar, [[https://progressives.house.gov/_cache/files/5/5/5523c5cc-4028-4c46-8ee1-b56c7101c764/B7B3674EFB12D933EA4A2B97C7405DD4.10-24-22-cpc-letter-for-diplomacy-on-russia-ukraine-conflict.pdf][send an open letter]] to Biden urging negotiations with Russia
  - The content of the letter is fairly anodyne but the timing and optics are bad
  - Letter urges Biden to open negotiations with Russia without necessarily involving Ukraine
  - Letter [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1584721381660336128][will be used by the Russians]] as evidence of American disunity, and will make Putin more likely to prolong the war
- According to the chief of Ukrainian military intelligence, Russian forces are [[https://twitter.com/yarotrof/status/1584433824976449536][not preparing to withdraw]] from Kherson
  - Instead they're rotating non-essential troops out, and reinforcing with combat troops
  - Appear to be preparing to fight a battle for Kherson city
- Belarus has [[https://twitter.com/Flash_news_ua/status/1584640515185573888][withdrawn the equipment]] that it deployed to the Ukrainian border and returned it to the bases where it was permanently stored
- An [[https://twitter.com/wartranslated/status/1584645449734328320][intercepted call]] from a Russian soldier describes life on the front lines
  - Says that his unit doesn't have enough armor-piercing ammunition and that the regular ammunition does nothing against Ukrainian Kevlar vests
  - Describes almost getting hit by a Ukrainian mortar strike; says that he has no idea how the Ukrainians managed to see his unit, didn't spot any drones in the area
  - Says that, from what he can see, the supply situation is much better for the Ukrainians especially with regards to drones
  - Says that none of the humanitarian donations that civilians are gathering in Russia is making it out to his unit on the front lines

  - The soldiers who carried out the mass shooting on October 16 were Tajik migrants who had been recruited under this program
- Ukrainian field commanders report that Shahed-136 loitering munitions are [[https://twitter.com/NeilPHauer/status/1583955590304641024][not a problem]]
  - /This makes sense, since Ukraine seems to have most of its short-range air defenses out in the field with its soldiers/
  - /Cities and fixed targets are protected by longer-range air defenses such as Buks and S-300s, which are comparatively less effective against small UAVs/
- Russia appears to be making a [[https://twitter.com/mjluxmoore/status/1583749669674307584][concerted effort]] to destroy Ukrainian electrical infrastructure

** 2022-10-20 Thursday
- /Content note: today's update is more focused on "big-picture" news, not directly related to the battlefield/
- /If you want battlefield news, just pretend that Russia attacked Bakhmutske, Soledar, Krasnohorivka and Nevelske again, like every other day/
- A Russian journalist [[https://twitter.com/ABarbashin/status/1583080281011277824][claims]] that the life expectancy of a Wagner contractor is just 9 days
- Russia's use of Iranian loitering munitions is [[https://www.washingtonpost.com/national-security/2022/10/20/russia-iran-kamikaze-drones/][allowing]] US intelligence to examine the wreckage, and devise ways of countering them
- The White House [[https://twitter.com/dsupervilleap/status/1583156576692510720][claims]] that Iranian troops are in Crimea, supporting Russian troops in the operation of loitering munitions
- The Ukrainian advance near Kharkiv has given Ukrainian troops a [[https://www.wsj.com/articles/ukraines-new-offensive-is-fueled-by-captured-russian-weapons-11664965264?redirect=amp][substantial amount]] of captured Russian armor and ammunition
  - Over the course of the entire war, photos on social media captured by Oryx have shown that Ukraine has captured
    - 460 main battle tanks
    - 92 self-propelled howitzers
    - 448 infantry fighting vehicles
    - 195 armored fighting vehicles
    - 44 MLRS
  - /That is a lot of tanks​/IFVs/
  - /This is approximately enough to outfit approximately *five* [[https://wiki.quanticle.net/Main/UnitedStatesArmoredBrigadeCombatTeam][US armored brigade combat teams]]/
  - /The US only has 10 armored brigade combat teams total/
- [[https://twitter.com/TadeuszGiczan/status/1582044513274822656][Thread]] on the presence of Russian troops in Belarus
  - Trains carrying troops are carrying just troops and some ancillary trucks and light transports, not armored vehicles
  - Troops are all newly mobilized conscripts
  - Deployed to existing military bases in northern Belarus, rather than near the Ukrainian border
  - From the above, we can conclude that the Russian troops in Belarus are new recruits sent to Belarussian bases for training, because Russian training facilities were overloaded
  - Therefore any threats by Putin and/or Lukashenko to open (re-open?) a northern front are likely bluffs at this time
  - In addition, Belarus is shipping its own tanks and armored vehicles to Russia --- this is not a thing that one would do if preparing for an imminent attack

  - Russians attacked [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0871584,37.5934123,11z][Pervomaiske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.9444825,37.5033277,11z][Marinka]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.2481406,37.6891264,11z][Novokalynove]]
    - /Haven't seen any direct attacks on Avdiivka in some time/
    - /Novokalynove is a new town to come under attack, but it's near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0095154,37.467888,11z][Krasnohorivka]]/
  - Russians also [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1582790998114959360][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.8534122,37.4742253,11z][Novomykhailivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.057244,37.5736284,14z][Nevelske]], and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0959777,37.719841,11z][Opytne]]
- Russian sources [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1582661267197612032][are claiming]] that Ukraine is advancing on [[https://www.google.com/maps/@46.8413911,33.4118719,11z][Beryslav]], in Kherson Oblast
  - /It's not clear what this means, or if these sources are accurate/
  - /The last confirmed report of Ukrainian positions in the Kherson area had them around [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.0660194,33.6276647,11z][Mylove]], which is significantly north of Beryslav/
  - /So this might mean that Ukraine has launched an attack in the direction of Beryslav from Mylove, without necessarily indicating that Ukrainians have advanced to Beryslav/
- Russia has [[https://twitter.com/WarInUkraineYet/status/1582703663445078017][declared martial law]] in the occupied regions of Kherson, Zaporizhzhia, Luhansk and Donetsk
  - /Not sure what this means; as I understand it, these areas were already largely under military authority/
  - [[https://twitter.com/AlexKokcharov/status/1582720631241551873][More details]] on the martial law declaration
    - In addition to declaring martial law in the occupied areas of Ukraine, Russia has implemented a 3-part alert system for Russia itself
    - Areas bordering Ukraine
      - "Average reaction level"
      - Local governments are instructed to
        - Implement entry/exit controls
        - Inspect transport vehicles (i.e. roadblocks and checkpoints)
        - Temporarily relocate residents to safe locations (/not sure what this means/)
        - Assert control over transportation and communications infrastructure and make it available to the Ministry of Defense
    - Areas east of those directly bordering Ukraine (includes Moscow)
      - "Elevated alert level"
      - Local authorities are to
        - Inspect transport vehicles
        - Assert control over transport and communications infrastructure
    - The remainder of the country is classified as "Basic alert level", and local authorities are required to be on alert, more or less
    - The upshot of this is that as one gets closer to Ukraine, one faces greater and greater restrictions on movement and increased inspections

  - Iran will reportedly be sending the Fateh-110 and Zolfaghar SRBMs

  - Crotale air defense systems
  - CAESAR artillery systems
  - MLRS (specific system to be decided)

  - /The Shahed-131 is a smaller drone with a shorter range and a smaller warhead/

  - /A real vote of confidence in the Russian military's ability to hold Kherson/

** 2022-10-11 Tuesday
- [[https://twitter.com/COUPSURE/status/1579465601231507457][Footage]] of a Russian cruise missile hitting Kyiv
- More HIMARS systems are [[https://twitter.com/oleksiireznikov/status/1579935298225831937][arriving]] in Ukraine
  - Ukrainian commanders [[https://www.wsj.com/articles/himars-transform-battle-for-ukraine-modern-warfare-11665169716][emphasize]] the importance of HIMARS
- Conscripts in Bryansk, one of the Russian Army's primary staging areas, are [[https://twitter.com/kromark/status/1579878847662915584][reportedly refusing]] to go to Ukraine
  - However, other recruits from the area deny that there is any large-scale refusal to go across the border
  - Recruits are often keeping their phones with them, leading to operational security breaches
  - Many rumors about high attrition rates
- A Finnish explosives expert [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1579480666282287104][analyzes]] the Kerch Bridge explosion
  - Notes the sparks the explosion set off as a sign of the potential use of thermite or other metallic incendiaries
  - Calls out the lack of a waterspout and the presence of scorch marks on top of the bridge as indicating the explosion occurred above the bridge
  - The truck that probably exploded [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1579511852815781888][might have exploded early]]
    - Would have been more destructive if the explosion had occurred in the center of the bridge
    - An explosion in the center would have destroyed both road segments and debris might have blocked the shipping channel running underneath
- The missile barrage fired at Ukraine [[https://twitter.com/HoansSolo/status/1579862659838902273][included]] 48N6 missiles from the S-300 air defense system
  - /Further evidence of Russian scrounging/
  - /Though, it is interesting that they're using anti-aircraft missiles in this role when the Ukrainian air-force is still flying/
- The first German IRIS-T air defense system [[https://twitter.com/Archer83Able/status/1579855431568347136][arrives]] in Ukraine

  - /The first overall commander was Dvornikov/
  - /Dvornikov was replaced by Zhidko/
  - /And now Zhidko has been replaced by Surovkin/
- Visually confirmed Ukrainian vehicle losses [[https://twitter.com/oryxspioenkop/status/1578851668640555008][exceed 1000]]
  - In comparison, Russian losses [[https://www.oryxspioenkop.com/2022/02/attack-on-europe-documenting-equipment.html][exceed 6000]]

  - /This is why the Ukrainians need tanks/
  - /It's great that they have Humvees, but tanks and IFVs would have been even more effective in this situation/
- Mobilization
  - There are reports of [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1577058010790129665][brawls]] between newly mobilized conscripts and existing contract servicemen
  - Mobilized servicemen in Omsk [[https://twitter.com/Andrew__Roth/status/1577562406733193218][asking when they'll be paid]], and being told that local officials don't actually have the money to pay them
  - /I see the Russian mobilization is going well, with zero problems/
- [[https://twitter.com/kromark/status/1577676812729176066][More information]] about the so-called "nuclear weapons" unit
  - Apparently this is a unit charged with carrying out "classified" tasks for the Russian military
  - As a result, it has less scrutiny, and, Russia being Russia, has an even higher level of corruption

  - Russia will be formally annexing Kherson, Zaporizhzhia, Donetsk and Luhansk Oblasts
  - This undoes the decisions made by Soviet rulers which went against the will of the Soviet people
  - While the Soviet Union cannot be restored, the mistakes made during its dissolution can be undone
  - The status of the annexed territories is not open to negotiation
  - The West is plotting to break up Russia, just as it plotted to break up the Soviet Union
  - Long rant enumerating various examples of Western imperialism
  - Accusation that the US was responsible for the sabotage of the Nord Stream pipelines
  - Suggestion that Russia is fighting for "traditional" family values --- says that Russia is fighting to keep families headed by a mother and a father, not "parent 1" and "parent 2"
  - Western sanctions are an effort to "cancel" Russia
  - Invites representatives from Luhansk, Donetsk, Zaporizhzhia and Kherson on stage to sign annexation documents

  - Admits that he doesn't know where, specifically, they'll be deployed
  - Also says that he doesn't know their equipment situation
  - Says that soldiers will be inspected by medical staff for conditions like poor vision and hernias, but emphasizes that these are not disqualifying conditions; says that he takes a bunch of pills every day himself

  - /Does that mean that Shandryholove has been liberated too?/

  - /I'm assuming that [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.1703532,37.7204702,11z][Karpivka]] has been liberated too, based on all the towns surrounding it having been liberated/
  - /Things are really starting to look bad for the Russians in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9852413,37.793474,11z][Lyman]]/
- Heavy fighting [[https://twitter.com/TCG_CrisisRisks/status/1574619122100367360][reported]] east of Siversk, near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.875291,38.2742613,11z][Zolotarivka]]
- Near Bakhmut, Russia [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1574807091373555713][launched a series of attacks all across the front line]]
  - [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4682884,37.9557667,11z][Kurdyumivka]]
  - [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.5266427,38.0582073,11z][Zaitseve]]
  - [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6605513,38.0876815,11z][Bakhmutske]]
  - [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6969192,38.0538431,11z][Soledar]]
  - [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.80505,38.1499134,11z][Vyimka]]
  - [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.8075094,38.2507431,11z][Spirne]]
  - Most of these attacks were unsuccessful, but there were reports of Russians making some progress near Kodema
- Russia [[https://twitter.com/TCG_CrisisRisks/status/1574619078051786752][hit the airports]] in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.0536614,33.2145245,12z][Kryvyi Rih]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.7049336,37.6273756,13z][Kramatorsk]], causing some damage and disruption
- In a first, Ukrainian aircraft [[https://twitter.com/TCG_CrisisRisks/status/1574619102655655937][conducted more sorties]] than Russian aircraft, possibly indicating maintenance disruptions caused by sanctions
- Ukrainian special forces or Ukrainian-supporting partisan forces [[https://twitter.com/TCG_CrisisRisks/status/1574619113770471425][destroyed a Russian supply train]] in Luhansk Oblast
- /TCG​_CrisisRisks has been reporting for some time how that Ukraine has been [[https://twitter.com/TCG_CrisisRisks/status/1574619129654300672][making progress with a counteroffensive]] east of Zaporizhzhia, but I haven't seen reporting of this anywhere else/
  - /That said, that area is mostly open terrain, so the Ukrainians may have made progress without necessarily liberating any towns, which is what tends to get reported/
- [[https://twitter.com/OAlexanderDK/status/1574740690877177858][Footage]] of the gas leaks from the Nord Stream 1 and 2 pipelines
  - Reportedly Swedish and Danish seismographs recorded explosions shortly before leaks in the pipelines were reported
  - Indicates possible sabotage
  - /But why would Russia or Europe sabotage the pipeline?/
  - /Russia benefits from keeping the pipeline intact, so that if Europe blinks on its sanctions, the pipeline remains ready to ship gas/
  - /Europe notably didn't sanction Nord Stream 1 after the war began, that pipeline was shut down on the Russian side/
- Putin's draft
  - Local authorities are reporting that draft-eligible people waiting in line at the Russia-Georgia border checkpoint are [[https://twitter.com/maxseddon/status/1574789264935632896][being served with recruitment notices]] in their cars
  - Similar scenes at the Finnish border, as eyewitneses report that people whose names were on mobilization lists were being [[https://twitter.com/akihheikkinen/status/1574706240093130752][detained]]
  - Kazakh authorities have stated that they [[https://twitter.com/maxseddon/status/1574679574935486464][will not extradite]] anyone fleeing there to escape conscription
  - [[https://twitter.com/kromark/status/1574707928313270272][Thread]] about a mobilized Russian soldier who was reportedly being sent to the front without any training at all

- Thread on the [[https://twitter.com/YudinGreg/status/1573765813294825472][scale and impact]] of mobilization
  - Mostly ethnic minorities being summoned
  - Fewer people being drafted from Moscow
  - University students being given deferments
  - /This is looking very much like the US draft in Vietnam/
- Footage of a Russian Su-30SM with its [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1573685526191902720][starboard engine on fire]] after it was hit by a Ukrainian MANPAD; the plane reportedly crashed later

- The Russian General Staff stated that the 120,000 conscripts currently serving [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1573780019226230786][will not be sent to the conflict zone and will not be re-mobilized after their term of enlistment had ended]]
- Many reports of people with health problems or no prior military experience could be [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1573820811999412226][attributed]] to chaos rather than malice
  - /Seems like local offices, especially those far from Moscow and St. Petersburg are recruiting everyone in an attempt to meet their quotas as fast as possible and are [[https://twitter.com/meduza_en/status/1573647201611513859][relying on downstream processing centers]] to filter out those who are unfit for service/
  - /This also might serve as cover for skipping individuals who are politically connected, etc, by sending old and sick people in their place, knowing that they'll get filtered out, but the quota will still have been met/
- Apparently mobilized soldiers will [[https://twitter.com/KofmanMichael/status/1573321104273428480][get two weeks of training]]

** 2022-09-21 Wednesday
- *Putin [[https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/russias-partial-mobilisation-will-see-300000-drafted-defence-minister-2022-09-21/][orders a partial mobilization]]*
  - [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1572554898201538561][Rob Lee's analysis]]
  - [[https://twitter.com/KofmanMichael/status/1572573086490464256][Michael Kofman's analysis]]
- [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.9852413,37.793474,11z][Lyman]] [[https://twitter.com/TCG_CrisisRisks/status/1572445137279782913][remains contested]]
  - Near Lyman, the Ukrainians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1572651422646243328][reportedly hold]] half of [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.0417742,37.7153533,11z][Drobysheve]]
- Russia [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1572651416077885440][launched another unsuccessful attack]] towards [[https://www.google.com/maps/@49.71005,37.61519,15z][Kupyansk]]
- Bakhmut area
  - Russian forces [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1572651428946251778][attacked]] [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.6605655,38.0876815,11z][Bakhmutske]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4682884,37.9557667,11z][Kurdyumivka]], [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4709235,38.0118927,12z][Mykolaivka Druha]] and [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.5266569,38.0582073,11z][Zaitseve]]
    - /This is the first attack reported _north_ of Bakhmut in some time/
    - /Russian forces seem to be making very slow progress south of Bakhmut, but still little or no progress to the north of the city/
- Russia [[https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/ukraine-tv-russia-has-released-some-fighters-taken-during-mariupol-battle-2022-09-21/][frees Azov Battalion members captured in Mariupol siege]] as part of a prisoner exchange
  - One of the prisoners exchanged was [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1572697479149240321][Viktor Medvedchuk]], reportedly the person Putin had picked to lead a puppet government
- Mark Hertling [[https://twitter.com/MarkHertling/status/1572571676524838915][has questions]] about how Russia will train and integrate its new recruits into its military
- Some local enlistment offices are saying that men will be [[https://twitter.com/PjotrSauer/status/1572664720901152773][sent to the front without training]]

*** [[https://geopolitics-decanted.simplecast.com/episodes/betting-it-all-on-black-putins-partial-mobilization-and-escalation-strategy-in-ukraine][2022-09-21 Geopolitics Decanted Podcast]]: "Betting It All On Black: Putin's Partial Mobilization"
- Host: Dmitry Alperovitch
- Panelists: Rob Lee, Michael Kofman
- Putin made a major announcement today, by enacting Russia's first mobilization since World War 2
- Up to 300,000 men will be inducted into the military, from a pool of 25 million with prior military experience
- Stop loss order: people currently serving on short term contracts will not be allowed to leave
- Refusing to serve has been criminalized
- Current conscripts will not currently be sent to the front line, but new recruits with prior military experience might be
- Reports of people already having received mobilization orders
- Mobilization will occur in a phased process
- The big open question is what is the ability of the Russian military to train, equip and organize this force?
- One thing to keep in mind is that the 300,000 number may not be reliable
  - Shoigu often quotes numbers that prove to be incorrect
- The Russian military no longer possesses the ability to integrate large numbers of untrained/lightly trained people like the Soviet military did
- Instead, at the start of this war, they had a force that was designed to be 2/3s contract servicemen, and 1/3 conscripts
- How many of the officers who were supposed to train and lead that 1/3 have been sent over to Ukraine already?
  - Unlike in the west, in Russia, training is not centralized
  - Troops show up to their unit, receive training, and serve out conscript duty with the unit
- Will be interesting to compare the performance of mobilized soldiers with the performance of the newly formed 3rd Army Corps
  - Third Army Corps is a formation that was created out of whole cloth and manned with volunteers who had signed up with short term contracts
  - Reportedly deployed to Kharkiv to try to stop the Ukrainian advance there
  - Still had issues with leadership and coordination
- The quantity and quality of the training that mobilized soldiers will receive is questionable
- Unit cohesion and morale will be questionable as well
- These measures will definitely help Russia in the short term
  - In some cases recently, you had 20-40% of units refusing to fight --- now refusing to fight is a criminal offense punishable by up to 15 years in prison
  - The forthcoming annexation of territory in Luhansk, Donetsk, Zaporizhzhia and Kherson potentially opens the way for Russia's existing conscripts to be deployed there
  - Stop-loss prevents contract servicemen from leaving
- But are these solutions tenable beyond the next 3-6 months?
- The Russian military has done most things poorly thus far; why we do we believe they'll handle mobilization better than anything else they've attempted to do?
- The mobilization announcement seems very hasty --- lots of details left unclear
- Calling newly mobilized troops "reservists" is an exaggeration --- these are civilian veterans
- Does this mobilization improve Putin's prospects for capturing the remainder of the Donbas?
  - Unclear
  - It was apparent after the Ukrainian counteroffensive around Izyum and Kharkiv that the Russian ability to capture the remainder of the Donbas was pretty much nil
  - Putin had to pick between three bad options
    - Retrenchment --- retreat from e.g. Kherson in order to concentrate more forces in Donetsk and Luhansk
      - Probably the least risky option
      - Russia has retrenched repeatedly in the past, and has maintained that its focus is on Donetsk and Luhansk
    - Mobilization
      - Political risks
      - Practical difficulties
    - Escalation
      - Not really an option that generates a path towards war termination
      - However, it was an option that could have bought time
- How will Russia deploy newly mobilized troops
  - Use them piecemeal to restore existing battalions to full strength
    - Soldiers aren't interchangeable parts that you can just plug and play
    - Ideally one would be rotating units off the front line in order to integrate replacements, but it's not clear that the Russians have the ability to do that
  - Organize new troops along the lines of Donetsk and Luhansk People's Republic Militias
    - Infantry-heavy formations with some motorization
    - Not very useful as a maneuver force, but can be used to garrison parts of the front lines and prevent further collapse
  - Create new maneuver units
    - Most effective use of new troops, but also the most complicated and time consuming
    - Maybe use the 3rd Army Corps as a model?
- Russia can fix the issues they had with the quantity of soldiers they'd deployed but it's not clear that they have the ability to fix the issues with the quality of soldiers
  - Best equipment has already been deployed, and, in many cases, destroyed
  - Likewise with experienced troops who could have mentored newly mobilized recruits
  - Morale problems are only going to get worse
  - Stop-loss policy allows the Russian military to force refuseniks to fight, but some proportion of them will choose to desert rather than continue
- Mobilization extends the war, but it's unclear how much it pushes the final outcome into Russia's favor
- What mobilization does do is increase the political risks for Putin
- Putin and Shoigu both emphasized the size of the front line in their respective announcements
- Stated that newly mobilized troops would be used to defend already captured territory rather than conduct new offensive operations
- Is a sign that Putin has realized that Russia is losing the war, and that his military won't be able to grind down the Ukrainian army over the long term
- Russia has another constraint that mobilization does little to solve: logistics and coordination
  - Does Russia have the command and control capacity to coordinate many more troops than it already has in the field?
  - Does Russia have the logistical capacity to supply additional forces in the field, especially in the face of a concerted Ukrainian effort to degrade Russian logistical capacity?
    - /Of course, one thing that Russia could do is use these newly mobilized troops to address its logistical shortfalls/
    - /You don't need much training to drive a military truck if you have experience driving trucks in the civilian world/
- The catalyst for this decision may have been the retaking of territory inside Luhansk Oblast by Ukraine
  - Russia has maintained since March 25 that the goal of the invasion was the liberation of Donetsk and Luhansk
  - Could talk their way around reversals near Kyiv, Kharkiv and Kherson
  - No way to talk their way out of losing territory in Luhansk
- Putin has no clear strategy for conflict termination
- Seems to be hoping that if he can just drag the war on for long enough, foreign diplomatic and military assistance to Ukraine will taper off and Ukraine will stop fighting
- The decision to mobilize is another sign of the myopia of Russian leadership --- make decisions that keep the war going for the next few months without regard for what happens after
- Over time, the Russian military has deprofessionalized and the Ukrainian military has professionalized
  - Most of Russia's best trained and best equipped forces (i.e. those with experience from Syria or Chechnya) have already been deployed
  - The forces replacing them have been progressively less experienced and less well equipped
  - On the other hand, Ukraine's forces have been receiving training in the UK and have been increasingly armed with better Western weapons
- What are the prospects for nuclear escalation?
  - Russia might threaten nuclear escalation to defend annexed territory
  - This is ill-judged because it raises questions about Russian willingness to use nuclear weapons to defend Crimea
  - The decision to use nuclear weapons will always be a political one
  - We can look at [[https://wiki.quanticle.net/Main/EscalationManagementAmpNuclearEmploymentInRussianMilitaryStrategy][Russian nuclear doctrine]], but Putin can disregard doctrine
  - Probability of nuclear escalation is still low, but even low probabilities can be unacceptable --- declassified sources report that the Soviets believed that the prospect for nuclear escalation during the Berlin Crisis was 5%, and this was judged to be unacceptable
- Does Russia have enough equipment to outfit mobilized troops
  - Equipment shouldn't be a problem --- Russia has lots of old stuff laying around that can be put to good use
  - /There are questions about maintenance, however --- not all of that old stuff may be still in usable condition/
  - Equipment is less of a problem than trained manpower --- driving a tank or APC is not the same as driving a car or a truck
  - How will these new recruits be trained on the equipment they will be expected to use?
  - Where will their officers come from?
- How effective will these new recruits be with two weeks of training
  - Depends on who, exactly, they're calling up
  - If we take Shoigu's 300,000 number, and the calculation behind it, at face value, there is no way that a majority of the newly mobilized troops will have prior experience as _contract_ soldiers
  - Most Russian conscripts weren't well trained to begin with, so it's an open question how much military skills someone with a year of conscript service 5+ years ago has
  - Will be really hard to replace lost technical skills
- Once again, it's useful to contrast this with Ukraine, whose soldiers are getting four week training rotations in the UK, along with coaching from American, British and other western technical experts
- How dangerous are these moves for Putin, politically?
  - Putin is increasingly and deliberately painting himself into a corner
  - Annexation, especially, is a point of no return --- can't use annexed territory as a bargaining chip any more
  - Mobilization is also a de facto point of no return --- Russia is now on a wartime footing, even if war has not legally been declared
  - Putin is staking the survival of his government on this war
- Existing analytical frameworks for Russia are not very useful any more
  - Few Russia watchers alive have seen a Russian mobilization
  - We are in almost uncharted waters
- The biggest question for Ukraine is, how does their economy keep functioning as the war drags on?

  - Russians [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1571917608278196224][may have had some success]] near [[https://www.google.com/maps/@48.4682884,37.9557667,11z][Kurdyumivka]]
    - /This is possibly worrying because it allows the Russians to link up their offensives out of Horlivka and Kodema/
- Kherson
  - Shelling [[https://twitter.com/DefMon3/status/1571926958266540033][was reported]] in [[https://www.google.com/maps/@47.0780615,32.8027841,11z][Snihurivka]]
- US defense officials say that supplying tanks to Ukraine [[https://twitter.com/JackDetsch/status/1571949385080254465][is being considered]], but it would depend on Ukraine being able to maintain and sustain them
- Germany is [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1571870185895723010][sending another 4 PzH 2000 self-propelled howitzers]] to Ukraine
- Rob Lee [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1571843782378749952][asks more questions]] about Russia's command structure in Ukraine
  - Argues that Wagner has been tasked with a single objective: gain territory near Bakhmut
  - So that is what they're doing, even as Russian lines collapse elsewhere
  - This is because it's likely that Wagner is operating outside the normal Russian chain of command, possibly reporting directly to Putin himself
- Rob Lee writes about [[https://twitter.com/RALee85/status/1571810517466980352][Ukraine's advantages]]
  - Manpower
  - Ability to learn and adapt
  - Interior lines
  - Unified command and control (/see above re: Wagner, and see below re: Luhansk and Donetsk People's Republic militias being outside the Russian chain of command/)
  - Clear goals (/though the fullest extent of those goals, esp. the liberation of Crimea, may not be achievable/)
  - Precision strike
  - Morale
  - Ability to strike behind enemy lines with resistance forces
  - Access to NATO and commercial satellite intelligence
- US troops are [[https://twitter.com/HoansSolo/status/1571733291748978688][helping Ukrainians conduct maintenance remotely]]
  - Calls out the use of Starlink in facilitating this communication
- According to the BBC, the Russians have [[https://bbcrussian.substack.com/p/russia-elite-force-losses-in-ukraine][lost a disproportionate number of troops]] from their elite units
  - This speaks to the the low level of readiness among regular Russian forces
  - Elite counterterror and special forces units are being called upon to conduct routine combat patrols, jobs that regular infantry should be able to easily handle
- According to the USAF, Ukraine has [[https://www.politico.com/news/2022/09/19/ukraine-has-shot-down-55-russian-warplanes-00057569][shot down 55 Russian aircraft]] thus far
- Konrad Muzyka [[https://ridl.io/the-kharkiv-offensive-and-its-consequences/][analyzes the Kharkiv offensive]]
  - Ukraine's success took advantage of both short and long-term deficiencies on the Russian side
  - Long-term deficiencies
    - Entering the war at peacetime strength
    - Choosing to increase the number of units by reducing the number of soldiers in each unit
    - This meant that, without mobilization, many BTGs could only deploy 50-60% of their rated strength
      - /And, as Rob Lee and Michael Kofman have pointed out, this overall number obscures the fact that the deficiency was disproportionately concentrated among infantry/
      - /In other words, Russia's mobilization strategy relied on having a most of its vehicle operators as contract servicemen, and its line infantry as conscripts/
      - /When the invasion went ahead without mobilization, many of Russia's motor rifle battalions were severely short-staffed in the number of regular soldiers they could deploy/
      - /This prevented Russian forces from effectively exercising combined arms tactics, which hurt them severely against Ukrainian anti-tank squads early in the war/
    - Losses early in the war were among the best trained and highest readiness formations (/see BBC story above/)
    - This lack of manpower has affected Russia's tactics
      - Conduct artillery bombardments and follow it up with reconnaissance in force
      - If defenders are still holding on, retreat and bombard again
      - /Tactics that would be intimately familiar for British and French generals in World War 1/
    - The above approach can be effective
      - Worked to capture Popasna, and later Severodonetsk and Lysychansk
      - However it is extremely inefficient and slow
      - Allows defenders ample time to establish secondary lines of defense, as the Ukrainians did at Bakhmut and Siversk after being driven from Severodonetsk and Lysychansk
    - This approach stands in stark contrast to the Ukrainian approach during the counteroffensive near Kharkiv, where mobile reconnaissance forces prevented the Russians from establishing secondary lines of defense
    - Another long-term deficiency is sustainment
      - There were a lot of Russian vehicles at Izyum when it was captured
      - Speaks to deficiencies in Russia's ability to repair vehicles and return them to the front lines in a timely manner
  - Short-term mistakes
    - Russian forces were not sufficient to secure the entire front
    - Faced with a choice
      1. Continue offensive operations out of Izyum, towards Slovyansk
      2. Continue offensive operations near Bakhmut
      3. Reinforce Kherson against a Ukrainian counterattack
    - Russian generals chose to allocate forces towards options 2 and 3, stripping reserves from Izyum
    - This lack of reserves near Izyum was apparent even in open-sources, showing up as a distinct decrease in Russian operational tempo
    - It's unclear whether Russian commanders didn't notice the build-up Ukrainian of Ukrainian forces in Kharkiv or whether they underestimated Ukraine's ability to field and coordinate such a large formation
  - Future implications
    - Unlikely that the Russian military will be able to rebuild its strength to threaten Ukrainian gains in the near future
    - Kyiv has seized the initiative
    - Ukraine has been able to trade territory for time, and time is on Ukraine's side
- Thread on the [[https://twitter.com/ChrisO_wiki/status/1570169288849326082][culture of institutionalized lying]] in the Russian military

  - /This was a major concern for NATO during the Cold War, and it was never adequately addressed/

** 2022-09-14 Wednesday
- Kharkiv
